# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Implementation and Privacy Guarantees for Scalable Keyword Search on SOLID-based Decentralized Data with Granular Visibility Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22100)
*Mohamed Ragab,Faria Ferooz,Mohammad Bahrani,Helen Oliver,Thanassis Tiropanis,Alexandra Poulovassilis,Adriane Chapman,George Roussos*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: ESPRESSO是一个去中心化框架，支持在Solid个人数据存储（pod）之间进行可扩展的关键词搜索，同时通过用户定义的可见性策略保护隐私。本文提出了一个正式威胁模型，分析索引和元数据生成、聚合及使用过程中的安全与隐私风险，并识别出限制元数据暴露、防止未授权推理的关键设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Solid等去中心化个人数据生态系统中，数据分布在众多pod中且受用户特定访问约束，导致搜索变得复杂。现有方案缺乏对隐私保护下的分布式搜索支持，亟需一种既能实现可扩展搜索又能保障用户隐私的框架。

Method: 提出ESPRESSO去中心化搜索框架，在pod内构建WebID作用域的索引，并采用隐私感知元数据实现跨服务器的源选择和排序。同时，设计了一个形式化威胁模型，分析索引与元数据在生成、聚合及使用过程中的安全隐私风险。

Result: 识别出包括元数据意外泄露和对手推断个人数据存储中敏感信息在内的风险；提出了限制元数据暴露并缓解未授权推理的关键设计原则。

Conclusion: 该威胁模型为评估隐私保护的去中心化搜索提供了基础，并为设计具有更强隐私保障的系统提供了指导方向。

Abstract: In decentralized personal data ecosystems grounded in architectures such as Solid, users retain sovereignty over their data via personal online data stores (pods), hosted on Solid-compliant server infrastructures. In such environments, data remains under the control of pod owners, which complicates search due to distribution across numerous pods and user-specific access constraints. ESPRESSO is a decentralized framework for scalable keyword-based search across distributed Solid pods under user-defined visibility policies. It addresses key challenges of decentralized search by constructing WebID-scoped indexes within pods and employing privacy-aware metadata to enable efficient source selection and ranking across servers. This paper further introduces a formal threat model for ESPRESSO, analysing the security and privacy risks associated with the generation, aggregation, and use of indexes and metadata. These risks include unintended metadata leakage and the potential for adversaries to infer sensitive information about data that resides within personal data stores. The analysis identifies key design principles that limit metadata exposure while mitigating unauthorized inference. The proposed threat model provides a foundation for evaluating privacy-preserving decentralized search and informs the design of systems with stronger privacy guarantees.

</details>


### [2] [MCI: A Maximal Clique Index for Efficient Arbitrary-Filtered Approximate Nearest Neighbor Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22171)
*Xiaowei Ye,Rong-Hua Li,Guoren Wang,Kaiwen Xue,Daiyin Wang,Xubin Li*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出了基于最大团索引（MCI）的图结构方法，用于高效处理带任意过滤谓词的近似最近邻搜索（AFANNS），通过最大团覆盖和局部邻域图几何致密化两大技术，在保证高召回率的同时大幅提升查询吞吐量并降低存储开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AFANNS方法在存储和计算上开销过大，缺乏既能保持高压缩率又能维持良好连通性的索引结构。

Method: (1) 最大团覆盖（MCC）：利用高维空间几何传递性，将密集邻域编码为最大团，实现高压缩和高连通性；(2) 局部邻域图几何致密化：从稀疏初始NNG出发，逐步增大距离阈值以局部致密化结构，恢复全局连通性；采用无锁并行构建和多种子查询策略。

Result: 在10个数据集上，MCI在高召回率下QPS优于SOTA方法一个数量级，空间占用显著更小，在范围/关键词过滤任务上也表现出竞争力。

Conclusion: MCI是一种通用且高效的AFANNS索引方案，兼顾了压缩、连通性和查询性能，具有鲁棒的泛化能力。

Abstract: Approximate Nearest Neighbor Search with arbitrary filtering predicates (AFANNS) is essential for modern data applications, yet existing methods often incur substantial storage and computational costs. In this work, we introduce the Maximal Clique Index (\mci), a novel graph-based index designed for robust and efficient AFANNS. The core idea of \mci is to approximate a dense Nearest Neighbor Graph (NNG) through a compact, clique-based representation. We propose two key techniques: (1) Maximal Clique Cover (\mcc), which exploits the geometric transitivity of high-dimensional spaces to encode dense neighborhoods as maximal cliques, achieving an index with high compression and connectivity; and (2) Local Neighborhood Graph Geometric Densification, a strategy that constructs an index approximating a large NNG from a sparse initial NNG, recovers global connectivity by progressively increasing distance thresholds to locally densify the structure. The index is built in a lock-free parallel manner for scalability and queried via a carefully-designed multi-seed strategy to handle fragmented predicate-induced subgraphs. Extensive experiments on 10 datasets show that \mci significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods by up to one order of magnitude in QPS at high recall while using substantially smaller space, and remains competitive even on range/keyword filtering tasks, demonstrating robust general-purpose performance.

</details>


### [3] [A Model-Driven Approach to Database Migration with a Unified Data Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22415)
*María J. Ortín,José R. Hoyos,Jesus García-Molina*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出基于U-Schema统一数据模型的泛用数据库迁移方法，通过中间表示降低异构模型间转换复杂度，实验验证了从关系到文档数据库迁移的可行性与语义保持能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据库迁移方法多为特定源-目标组合设计，在支持多种异构数据模型（如关系型与NoSQL）的通用场景下存在局限性。

Method: 以U-Schema作为统一中间表示（pivot model），分别定义各数据模型到U-Schema的映射，将N×M种变换缩减为N+M种；在模式转换过程中生成追踪信息，用于解耦地指导后续数据迁移。

Result: 在模式级验证中实现高结构保持率；生成的文档模式与设计意图一致；在查询行为（连接、聚合、嵌套结构）上保持语义正确性；性能测试表明该方法对递增数据规模可行。

Conclusion: 虽然实验聚焦于关系型到文档型（如Northwind基准）的迁移，但该方法框架本身支持多种数据模型，具有良好的泛用扩展性。

Abstract: Database migration is a key task in software modernization, increasingly involving transformations across heterogeneous data models such as relational and NoSQL systems. Existing approaches are typically designed for specific source-target combinations, which limits their applicability in multi-model environments.
  This paper proposes a generic database migration approach based on the U-Schema unified data model, which acts as a pivot representation. By defining mappings between each data model and U-Schema, the approach reduces the number of required transformations and enables schema conversion across heterogeneous paradigms. Trace information is generated during schema transformation to capture correspondences between source and target elements, and is subsequently used to guide data migration in a decoupled manner.
  The approach has been implemented and evaluated through experiments covering schema-level validation, data-level semantic preservation, and performance analysis. The results show that the migration pipeline achieves high structural preservation under round-trip reconstruction, produces document schemas consistent with the intended design decisions, and preserves query behavior across a variety of access patterns, including joins, aggregations, and nested structures. Performance results demonstrate the feasibility of the approach for datasets of increasing size.
  The evaluation focuses on relational-to-document migration using both synthetic datasets and the Northwind benchmark. While this scenario provides a concrete instantiation, the approach is designed to support multiple data models within a unified framework.

</details>


### [4] [How Hard is it to Decide if a Fact is Relevant to a Query?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22422)
*Meghyn Bienvenu,Diego Figueira,Pierre Lafourcade*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文研究了数据库中对布尔合取查询的"事实相关性"问题的计算复杂性，发现自我连接是导致问题比查询评估更难的关键因素，并在禁止或限制自我连接时证明了相关性与查询评估具有相同的复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管事实相关性对查询答案解释至关重要，但其组合复杂性尚未得到详细研究，哪些因素导致问题困难以及哪些限制能降低复杂度尚不明确。

Method: 通过复杂性理论分析，识别自我连接作为关键障碍，证明禁止或限制自我连接时相关性复杂度降至与查询评估相同（NP或LogCFL）；在本体查询场景中引入"交互宽度"概念推广自我连接宽度。

Result: 证明了CQs的查询相关性是Σ^p_2-complete；链式CQs（即使无环）已是NP-hard；禁止/限制自我连接时复杂度降至NP（无结构限制）或LogCFL（有界超树宽类）；本体查询中限制交互宽度可同样降低复杂度。

Conclusion: 明确了使相关性比查询评估更困难的核心因素是自我连接，识别出了可高效计算相关性的自然查询类别。

Abstract: We consider the following fundamental problem: given a database D, Boolean conjunctive query (CQ) q, and fact f in D, decide whether f is relevant to q wrt. D, i.e., does f belong to a minimal subset S of D such that S |= q. Despite being of central importance to query answer explanation, the combined complexity of deciding query relevance has not been studied in detail, leaving open what makes this problem hard, and which restrictions can yield lower complexity. Relevance has already been shown to be harder than query evaluation: namely, $Σ^p_2$-complete for CQs, even over a binary signature. We further observe that NP-hardness applies already to (acyclic) chain CQs. Our work identifies self-joins (multiple atoms with the same relation) as the culprit. Indeed, we prove that if we forbid or bound the occurrence of self-joins, then relevance has the same complexity as query evaluation, namely, NP (without structural restrictions) and LogCFL (for bounded hypertreewidth classes). In the ontology setting, we establish an analogous result for ontology-mediated queries consisting of a CQ and DL-Lite_R ontology, namely that relevance is no harder than query answering provided that we bound the interaction width (which generalizes both self-join width and a recently introduced 'interaction-free' condition). Our results thus pinpoint what makes relevance harder than query evaluation and identify natural classes of queries which admit efficient relevance computation.

</details>


### [5] [It's Time to Standardize RDF Messages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22619)
*Pieter Colpaert,Piotr Sowinski*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文提出RDF消息(RDF Message)概念，将RDF数据集视为原子性通信单元，解决流式场景中消息边界不明确导致的互操作性问题，并定义RDF消息流和消息日志，支持增量消费和可复现回放。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RDF语义和工具缺乏对"哪些陈述属于同一消息"的互操作定义，开发者依赖非标准技术、传输层假设或启发式方法，导致互操作性问题和效率低下。

Method: 提出RDF消息概念——将RDF数据集视为原子性通信单元，明确消息边界；在此基础上定义RDF消息流和消息日志；并引入RDF消息配置文件(如LDES、ActivityStreams)描述分页、结构、排序和保留策略。

Result: 实现了消息边界的跨序列化、传输和存储系统的显式化，支持增量消费和可复现回放，适用于物联网观测、归档RDF流、纳米出版物、SPARQL CONSTRUCT结果处理等场景。

Conclusion: 该提案为RDF流处理提供了标准化基础，目前正在W3C RDF流处理社区组寻求更广泛的支持和反馈。

Abstract: RDF-based systems increasingly operate in event-driven and streaming settings, where producers and consumers exchange data as discrete units of communication rather than as freely mergeable RDF statements. As existing RDF semantics and tooling do not provide an interoperable notion of what statements belong together as one message, developers often rely on out-of-standard techniques, transport-level assumptions, or heuristics, leading to interoperability problems and inefficiencies. We propose the concept of an RDF Message as an RDF Dataset intended to be interpreted atomically as a single communicative act, laying the foundation for defining RDF Message Streams and RDF Message Logs. The proposal makes message boundaries explicit across serializations, transport, and storage systems, which in turn enables incremental consumption and reproducible replay in use cases such as IoT observations, archived RDF streams, nanopublications, or processing SPARQL CONSTRUCT results. Building on this, RDF Message Profiles, such as Linked Data Event Streams or ActivityStreams, then provide the terms for describing pagination, message structure, ordering, or retention policies. As part of the W3C Community Group on RDF Stream Processing, we are now seeking broader support and comments on the proposal from the Semantic Web community.

</details>


### [6] [A dataset of early blockchain-registered AI agents on Ethereum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22652)
*Yulin Liu*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文构建了基于ERC-8004标准的区块链注册AI智能体结构化数据集，涵盖链上身份、交易、声誉及链下元数据，覆盖以太坊主网10,000个智能体，支持去中心化AI生态的实证研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有区块链与AI交叉领域缺乏标准化的智能体注册数据集，难以支撑对去中心化AI生态中智能体身份形成、声誉系统和服务暴露等问题的实证研究。

Method: 通过Web3 RPC从以太坊主网查询ERC-8004标准下的链上数据，结合解析的链下元数据，将身份记录、交易事件、声誉摘要和反馈记录处理为表格化数据格式。

Result: 构建了包含10,000个智能体的结构化数据集，涵盖事件级记录和聚合摘要，在定义的区块范围内覆盖完整的链上身份与交易信息。

Conclusion: 该数据集为区块链分析、去中心化信任基础设施以及新兴智能体经济的研究提供了可复现的数据资源，有助于理解早期去中心化AI生态系统的演化机制。

Abstract: This study presents a structured dataset of blockchain-registered artificial intelligence agents under the ERC-8004 standard on Ethereum. The dataset integrates on-chain identity records, minting transactions, transfer events, reputation summaries, and individual feedback records, together with resolved off-chain metadata where available. Data were collected from Ethereum mainnet using Web3 RPC queries and processed into tabular form to enable reproducible analysis. The dataset covers 10,000 agents within a defined block range and includes both event-level records and aggregated summaries. It enables empirical research on agent identity formation, reputation systems, service exposure, and early-stage decentralized AI ecosystems. This resource supports studies in blockchain analytics, decentralized trust infrastructure, and the emerging agentic economy.

</details>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Shard the Gradient, Scale the Model: Serverless Federated Aggregation via Gradient Partitioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22072)
*Amine Barrak*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出GradsSharding，一种将梯度张量分片（M片）的联邦学习聚合架构，每片由独立无服务器函数处理，突破传统树状聚合的内存上限瓶颈，支持任意大模型聚合且结果比特级一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无服务器FL架构（lambda-FL、LIFL）因每个聚合器需存储完整梯度，受限于无服务器平台的单函数内存上限（如AWS Lambda的10 GB），无法处理大模型梯度，存在硬性可扩展天花板。

Method: 将梯度张量划分为M个分片，每个分片由独立无服务器函数接收所有客户端贡献并独立求平均。利用FedAvg逐元素平均性质，确保与树状聚合比特级一致，模型精度不变。单函数内存占用为O(|θ|/M)，与客户端数量无关。

Result: 在HPC实验和真实AWS Lambda部署中对比lambda-FL和LIFL，模型规模从43 MB到5 GB。约500 MB梯度大小时出现成本交叉点，VGG-16规模下成本降低2.7倍，且是唯一能在无服务器内存上限之外部署的方案。

Conclusion: GradsSharding通过梯度分片策略彻底突破了无服务器FL的内存瓶颈，在大模型场景下具有显著的成本优势，且保证了模型精度的不变性。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) aggregation on serverless platforms faces a hard scalability ceiling: existing architectures (lambda-FL, LIFL) partition clients across aggregators, but every aggregator must hold the complete model gradient in memory. When gradients exceed the per-function memory limit (e.g., 10 GB on AWS Lambda), aggregation becomes infeasible regardless of tree depth or branching factor. We propose GradsSharding, which instead partitions the gradient tensor into M shards, each averaged independently by a serverless function that receives contributions from all clients. Because FedAvg averaging is element-wise, this produces bit-identical results to tree-based approaches, so model accuracy is invariant by construction. Per-function memory is bounded at O(|θ|/M), independent of client count, enabling aggregation of arbitrarily large models. We evaluate GradsSharding against lambda-FL and LIFL through HPC experiments and real AWS Lambda deployments across model sizes from 43 MB to 5 GB. Results show a cost crossover at approximately 500 MB gradient size, 2.7x cost reduction at VGG-16 scale, and that GradsSharding is the only architecture that remains deployable beyond the serverless memory ceiling.

</details>


### [8] [FlashSpread: IO-Aware GPU Simulation of Non-Markovian Epidemic Dynamics via Kernel Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22092)
*Heman Shakeri,Behnaz Moradi-Jamei,Aram Vajdi,Ehsan Ardjmand*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: FlashSpread是一个基于GPU的非马尔可夫（更新）流行病模拟框架，通过将整个每步更新流水线融合到单个Triton内核中，在A100 GPU上实现了8.09 Giga-NUPS的峰值吞吐量，比优化的CPU tau-leaping快217倍，并支持多达1亿节点规模的接触网络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准CPU方法在处理非马尔可夫流行病模拟时，由于年龄依赖的风险函数导致每步更新密集，使得稀疏事件队列策略失效，亟需高效的GPU加速方案。

Method: 将CSR遍历、erfcx-based hazard评估、Bernoulli tau-leaping、状态转移和下一时间步感染性回写整合为单个融合Triton内核，中间数据始终保留在流多处理器寄存器中；采用块标量跳过机制保持CUDA Graph捕获，以及度感知的CSR调度（线程/线程束/边合并）以保持规模自由图上的峰值吞吐量。

Result: 在N=10^6的均匀度图上达到8.09 Giga-NUPS，比优化的CPU tau-leaping快217倍；在Barabasi-Albert图上，基于合并的调度相比默认内核恢复4.5倍性能（0.45到2.0 Giga-NUPS）；在单张A100（40GB）上可扩展到N=10^8；混合精度存储路径将L2可访问规模扩展约3倍，在带宽受限端提供1.15倍吞吐量提升；与精确非马尔可夫Gillespie参考相比，结构偏差约为6%（峰值感染）和7%（最终攻击率）。

Conclusion: FlashSpread在GPU上实现了非马尔可夫流行病模拟的大规模加速，验证了融合内核设计在密集更新场景下的有效性，且偏差水平在流行病学参数不确定性范围内可接受。

Abstract: Non-Markovian (renewal) epidemic simulation on multi-million-node contact networks is essential for realistic forecasting under general age-dependent holding-time distributions (log-normal, Weibull, Erlang, and similar), but the age-dependent hazard forces dense per-step updates that render the sparse event-queue strategies of standard CPU methods ineffective. We present FlashSpread, a GPU framework that consolidates the per-step renewal pipeline (CSR traversal, numerically stable erfcx-based hazard evaluation, Bernoulli tau-leaping, state transition, and next-step infectivity write-back) into a single fused Triton kernel whose intermediates never leave streaming-multiprocessor registers, with block-scalar skips that preserve CUDA Graph capture and a degree-aware CSR dispatch (thread / warp / edge-merge) that keeps the peak throughput on scale-free graphs. On an NVIDIA A100 the fused CUDA-Graph engine reaches 8.09 Giga-NUPS at N = 10^6 on a uniform-degree graph, a 217x strict hardware speedup over optimised CPU tau-leaping at the same N; on a Barabasi-Albert graph of the same size the merge-based dispatch recovers 4.5x (0.45 to 2.0 Giga-NUPS) over the default kernel, and the framework scales to N = 10^8 on a single A100 (40 GB), with a mixed-precision storage path that extends the L2-reachable scale by roughly 3x and delivers a 1.15x throughput lift at the far bandwidth-bound end. Validation against an exact non-Markovian Gillespie reference shows a structural-bias floor of approximately 6% on peak infection and approximately 7% on final attack rate that does not detectably decrease as epsilon nears 0 across two decades of tolerance, comfortably within typical epidemiological parameter uncertainty. Code: https://github.com/Shakeri-Lab/FlashSpread.

</details>


### [9] [GICC: A High-Performance Runtime for GPU-Initiated Communication and Coordination in Modern HPC Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22126)
*Baodi Shan,Mauricio Araya-Polo,Barbara Chapman*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出GICC框架，让GPU核函数直接驱动NIC级跨节点协调，无需主机参与。在Slingshot上实现高达229x的延迟降低和25%的弱扩展效率提升，在InfiniBand上比NVSHMEM降低1.95x的put延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分布式GPU应用在跨节点协调方面缺乏内核级支持：OFI互连（如Slingshot）依赖主机驱动进度，缺乏回收预置NIC工作的有界机制；InfiniBand虽支持GPU发起通信，但存在不必要的同步和锁开销。

Method: GICC通过三个关键设计实现：(1) GPU核直接触发NIC级操作，无主机参与；(2) 将协调语义与数据移动解耦；(3) 引入异步资源回收机制，NIC同时通知GPU和主机内存，轻量级主机线程并发回收NIC资源，不向协调路径注入延迟。

Result: 在Slingshot上每协调延迟降低229x，弱扩展效率提升25%；在InfiniBand上put延迟比NVSHMEM低1.95x；在64 AMD MI250X GCDs上工业模板代理中，GPU感知MPI通信时间比GICC高52%，GICC并行效率42% vs MPI的35.4%。

Conclusion: GICC证明了GPU驱动跨节点协调的可行性，通过去主机化协调路径和异步资源回收，在主流GPU和互连上均实现显著性能提升，为未来分布式GPU运行时设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Distributed GPU applications increasingly rely on kernel-level, cross-node coordination to reduce launch overheads and improve compute-communication overlap, but such support is lacking. On OFI-based interconnects such as HPE Slingshot, which powers six of the top ten systems in the November 2025 Top500, including the top three, GPU kernels cannot autonomously drive distributed coordination: existing runtimes rely on host-driven progress and lack a bounded mechanism for recycling pre-staged NIC work across repeated GPU-triggered operations. On InfiniBand, GPU-initiated communication is possible, but current implementations incur unnecessary synchronization and locking overheads.
  This paper presents GICC, a framework that enables GPU kernels to directly trigger NIC-level operations without host involvement on the fast path. In stencils, GPU threads initiate halo exchanges as soon as boundary regions are computed, enabling fine-grained overlap between interior computation and boundary transfer. GICC decouples coordination semantics from data movement and introduces asynchronous resource reclamation: the NIC signals completion to both GPU and host memory, letting a lightweight host thread recycle NIC resources concurrently with GPU execution without injecting latency into the coordination path. This sustains GPU-driven coordination under finite NIC state, absent from existing OFI-based runtimes.
  We implement GICC on NVIDIA and AMD GPUs over InfiniBand and Slingshot. On Slingshot, GICC reduces per-coordination latency by up to 229x and improves weak scaling efficiency by up to 25%. On InfiniBand, it achieves up to 1.95x lower put latency than NVSHMEM by eliminating unnecessary locking and synchronization. On an industrial stencil proxy on 64 AMD MI250X GCDs, GPU-aware MPI incurs over 52% higher communication time than GICC, which achieves 42% parallel efficiency versus MPI's 35.4%.

</details>


### [10] [$O(K)$-Approximation Coflow Scheduling in $K$-Core Optical Circuit Switching Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22146)
*Xin Wang,Hong Shen,Hui Tian,Ye Tao*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究了多核光电路交换（OCS）网络中的协同流调度问题，提出了一种基于线性规划引导的全局排序、跨核流量分配和核内电路调度的算法，在非同时停止（异步）重配置模型下，实现了8K（零释放时间）和8K+1（任意释放时间）的近似比，其中K为OCS核心数。该框架同样适用于H核电分组交换（EPS）网络，分别提供4H和4H+1的近似保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注多核电分组交换（EPS）网络中的协同流调度，而对多核OCS网络的研究较少，且已有结果性能保证较差。本文旨在填补这一空白，解决多核OCS网络中跨核耦合（流量分配）与核内约束（端口独占性和重配置开销）两大挑战。

Method: 提出集成线性规划引导（LP-guided）全局协同流排序、跨核流量分配和核内电路调度的算法。针对非同时停止（异步）重配置模型，通过LP求解得到全局排序，再基于该排序进行跨核流量分配和核内电路调度，从而最小化加权总完成时间（CCT）。

Result: 在零释放时间下达到8K近似比，任意释放时间下达到8K+1近似比（K为OCS核心数）。该框架扩展到H核EPS网络时，分别提供4H和4H+1的近似保证。

Conclusion: 本文首次为多核OCS网络中的协同流调度提供了具有常数近似比保证的算法，并证明了所提框架可推广至EPS网络，具有较好的通用性。

Abstract: Coflow has emerged as a fundamental application-layer abstraction in distributed systems, representing communication dependencies and enabling collaborative management of related flows to enhance job completion efficiency. To meet the increasing bandwidth demands of modern data center networks (DCNs), optical circuit switches are widely deployed due to their high capacity and energy efficiency. Simultaneously, DCN deployments are evolving towards heterogeneous parallel architectures, where multiple independent optical circuit switching (OCS) cores operate concurrently to facilitate bandwidth expansion and incremental upgrades. However, existing research on coflow scheduling in multi-core switching fabrics primarily focuses on electrical packet switching (EPS) networks, with a few known results on OCS networks without or with a poor performance guarantee.
  This paper studies the coflow scheduling problem in multi-core OCS networks under the not-all-stop (i.e., asynchronous) reconfiguration model, focusing on two major challenges of overcoming cross-core coupling for inter-core traffic allocation and satisfying the constraints of port exclusivity and reconfiguration overhead for intra-core circuit scheduling. To minimize total weighted coflow completion time (CCT), we propose an efficient algorithm by integrating linear programming-guided (LP-guided) global coflow ordering, inter-core flow allocation and intra-core circuit scheduling that achieves approximation ratios of 8K and 8K+1 for zero and arbitrary release times of coflows, respectively, where K is the number of OCS cores. This framework is also applicable to H-core EPS networks, providing approximation guarantees of 4H and 4H+1 for zero-time and arbitrary-time release, respectively.

</details>

### [12] [Guess-Verify-Refine: Data-Aware Top-K for Sparse-Attention Decoding on Blackwell via Temporal Correlation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22312)
*Long Cheng,Ritchie Zhao,Timmy Liu,Mindy Li,Xianjie Qiao,Kefeng Duan,Yu-Jung Chen,Xiaoming Chen,Bita Darvish Rouhani,June Yang*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出Guess-Verify-Refine (GVR)，一种数据感知的精确Top-K算法，利用相邻解码步骤的时间相关性，通过猜测-验证-优化策略加速稀疏注意力解码中的Top-K选择，在Blackwell上实现了平均1.88x的算子加速比，端到端TPOT提升最高7.52%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在长上下文LLM服务中，稀疏注意力解码器依赖精确Top-K选择来挑选每个查询token最重要的key-value条目。即使索引器和注意力内核已经高度优化，每个解码查询都需要运行的Top-K阶段仍然成为显著的延迟瓶颈。

Method: GVR利用连续解码步骤间的时间相关性：将上一步的Top-K作为预测信号，计算预索引统计信息，通过正割法计数在1-2次全局遍历中缩小有效阈值范围，使用无竞争收集器验证候选，并在共享内存中完成精确选择。该方法利用了DeepSeek稀疏注意力索引器得分的Toeplitz/RoPE结构特性。

Result: 在集成到TensorRT-LLM的DeepSeek-V3.2真实工作负载上，GVR实现了平均1.88x的单算子加速比（最高2.42x），保持比特精确的Top-K输出。在TEP8最小延迟部署中，100K上下文长度下端到端TPOT提升最高7.52%，长上下文下收益更大。

Conclusion: GVR在Blackwell的TensorRT-LLM DSA栈上验证有效，其原理可推广至解码阶段Top-K具有时间稳定性的其他稀疏注意力解码器。

Abstract: Sparse-attention decoders rely on exact Top-K selection to choose the most important key-value entries for each query token. In long-context LLM serving, this Top-K stage runs once per decode query and becomes a meaningful latency bottleneck even when the indexer and attention kernels are already highly optimized. We present \textbf{Guess-Verify-Refine (GVR)}, a data-aware exact Top-K algorithm for sparse-attention decoding on NVIDIA Blackwell. GVR exploits temporal correlation across consecutive decode steps: it uses the previous step's Top-K as a prediction signal, computes pre-indexed statistics, narrows to a valid threshold by secant-style counting in 1-2 global passes, verifies candidates with a ballot-free collector, and finishes exact selection in shared memory. We connect this behavior to the Toeplitz / RoPE structure of DeepSeek Sparse Attention (DSA) indexer scores and validate the design on real DeepSeek-V3.2 workloads integrated into TensorRT-LLM. GVR achieves an average \textbf{1.88x} single-operator speedup over the production radix-select kernel, with up to \textbf{2.42x} per layer per step, while preserving bit-exact Top-K outputs. In controlled TEP8 min-latency deployment, it improves end-to-end TPOT by up to \textbf{7.52%} at 100K context, with larger gains at longer contexts and smaller but still positive gains under speculative decoding. While implemented and validated in the current TensorRT-LLM DSA stack on Blackwell, the same principle may extend to sparse-attention decoders whose decode-phase Top-K exhibits temporal stability.

</details>


### [13] [A comprehensive evaluation of spatial co-execution on GPUs using MPS and MIG technologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22430)
*Jorge Villarrubia,Luis Costero,Francisco D. Igual,Katzalin Olcoz*

Main category: cs.DC

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对NVIDIA的MPS（Multi-Process Service）和MIG（Multi-Instance GPU）两种空间共享技术进行全面评估和对比分析。

Result: MPS在最佳场景下性能提升30%、能耗降低20%，但在内存争用下性能下降约30%；MIG硬件隔离解决了内存争用，但开销更高且灵活度不足。

Abstract: To mitigate the increasingly common underutilization of computational resources in modern GPUs, spatial sharing methods enable multiple applications to use them simultaneously. This work presents a comprehensive evaluation of NVIDIA's primary technologies to achieve that goal: Multi-Process Service (MPS) and Multi-Instance GPU (MIG). Our findings reveal a crucial trade-off between MPS's flexibility and MIG's isolation, and provide many key insights for improving the co-execution strategy according to job profiles. In the most favorable scenarios, MPS improves performance by up to 30% and reduces energy by about 20%, using its provisioning option to avoid resource monopolization. However, under memory contention, it suffers severe degradation, worsening performance by around 30%. Conversely, MIG's full hardware isolation resolves memory contention, leading to more consistent improvements, but these gains are tempered by higher overhead, and its rigid scheme can degrade performance in certain cases.

### [14] [LaissezCloud: Continuous Resource Renegotiation for the Public Cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22509)
*Tejas Harith,Antoine Kaufmann*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: LaissezCloud提出了一种持续竞价、动态重协商的云资源管理平台，允许租户和运营商在线更新出价，实现资源分配的持续可竞争性，相比传统按需和竞价实例，在异构集群中将争用下的性能下降降低8-23%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公有云暴露异构硬件，但分配接口仍基于僵化的按需和竞价服务类，难以在过载、异构集群中同时满足租户的时变目标和运营商的约束，且不愿暴露内部状态。

Method: 提出持续可竞争分配机制：租户和运营商在线更新出价，运行中的租户仅当出价高于竞争需求时才保留资源；定价同时作为窄接口和激励对齐机制，运营商可在不暴露内部遥测数据的情况下引入功耗、冷却、碳约束等价格信号。

Result: 在多样化的加速器负载下，相比按需和竞价基线，将争用下的性能下降降低8-23%，并可扩展至至少10,000节点的集群规模。

Conclusion: 持续竞价与动态重协商机制能有效平衡租户与运营商在异构过载集群中的多样化需求，兼顾性能、可扩展性与隐私保护。

Abstract: Public clouds increasingly expose heterogeneous hardware, but their allocation interface remains built around rigid on-demand and spot service classes. This makes it hard to satisfy time-varying tenant objectives and operator constraints in oversubscribed, heterogeneous clusters without exposing internal application or infrastructure state. We present LaissezCloud, a cloud resource management platform for continuous re-negotiation of running allocations. Unlike spot instances, which use launch-time bids and unilateral preemption, LaissezCloud keeps allocations continuously contestable during execution: tenants and operators update bids online, and a running tenant keeps a resource only as long as its bid exceeds competing demand. Pricing serves both as a narrow waist and as an incentive-alignment mechanism between mutually untrusted participants: tenants express utility through bids, while operators price in power, cooling, or carbon constraints without exposing internal telemetry. Across a diverse set of accelerator workloads, LaissezCloud reduces performance degradation under contention by 8-23% versus on-demand and spot baselines, and scales to clusters of at least 10,000 nodes.

</details>

### [15] [Turnstile Streaming Algorithms Might (Still) as Well Be Linear Sketches, for Polynomial-Length Streams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22052)
*Cheng Jiang,Yinchen Liu,Huacheng Yu*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明了在多项式长度流中，任意使用S比特空间的turnstile算法都可以被模拟为线性草图（使用O(S)个线性测量），推翻了此前仅适用于指数长度流的结论，并基于傅里叶分析给出了新证明方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流式计算中一个基本问题是：是否每个节约空间的turnstile算法本质上都是线性草图？此前[LNW14]建立了等价性但要求流长度为双指数级（不现实），而[KP20]在线性长度流中给出了反例。最实际的多项式长度流是否成立一直悬而未决。

Method: 放弃传统的转移图机制，采用傅里叶分析框架和加性组合学工具。核心思路：证明任何S比特算法只能对低维晶格上的重傅里叶频率敏感，然后利用这些频率构造草图矩阵的行。

Result: 1) 多项式长度turnstile算法可被模拟为线性草图：从O(S)个线性测量中恢复输出，总空间O(S log S)。2) 对于平滑问题，在合适输入分布下，可得到O(S/log D)次测量和O(S)总空间的草图。3) 结果扩展至严格turnstile流和非均匀ROBP。4) 通过实值草图和通信下界得到多项式长度流的新下界。

Conclusion: 多项式长度流中，空间高效turnstile算法与线性草图之间确实存在等价性（以O(S)测量为代价），填补了此前指数流和线性流之间的空白。新的傅里叶分析方法为流式复杂性研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: A fundamental question in streaming complexity is whether every space-efficient turnstile algorithm is implicitly a linear sketch. The landmark work of Li, Nguyen, and Woodruff [LNW14] established an equivalence between the two, but their reduction requires a stream length that is at least doubly exponential in the dimension $n$. In the opposite direction, results by Kallaugher and Price [KP20] demonstrate a separation for streams of linear length, showing that the equivalence does not hold in general. The most natural and practically relevant regime -- polynomial-length streams -- has therefore remained open.
  We show that polynomial-length turnstile algorithms admit linear-sketch simulations. More precisely, if a turnstile algorithm uses $S$ bits of space and succeeds on all streams of length $\mathrm{poly}(D, n)$, then on final vectors $x$ with $\|x\|_2 \le D$, its output can be recovered from $O(S)$ linear measurements of $x$, using $O(S \log S)$ bits overall. For smooth problems under appropriate input distributions, a mollified version of the reduction yields a bounded-entry sketch with $O(S / \log D)$ measurements and optimal $O(S)$ total space. Our results extend to strict turnstile streams and non-uniform Read-Once Branching Programs (ROBPs).
  Our proof departs from prior transition-graph based machinery, relying instead on a Fourier-analytic framework and tools from additive combinatorics to extract discrete linear measurements. Our analysis shows that any $S$-bit algorithm can only be sensitive to a low-dimensional lattice of heavy Fourier frequencies, which we then use to construct the rows of the sketching matrix. Consequently, we obtain new lower bounds for polynomial-length streams via existing real sketching and communication lower bounds.

</details>


### [16] [Cuts and Gauges for Submodular Width](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22663)
*Matthias Lanzinger*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文从几何角度重新诠释了子模宽度（submodular width），将其与超图边分离的枝宽参数建立联系，并通过凸体的变分刻画，证明了子模宽度与广义 hypertree 宽度在多种自然条件下具有对数关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 子模宽度是衡量合取查询评估复杂性的关键结构度量，但现有理解多基于代数/组合视角。作者希望从几何角度重新诠释子模宽度，揭示其与图论概念（如线图树宽、多商品流）的内在联系，并探索其与广义 hypertree 宽度之间的精确关系。

Method: 1) 将子模宽度转化为基于超图边分离的枝宽参数（可达 3/2 近似）；2) 建立下界构造与"平衡边分离且诱导代价小"这一问题的等价关系；3) 通过凸体的变分刻画给出统一形式化表达；4) 连接线图树宽、多商品流等经典图论概念，推导子模宽度与广义 hypertree 宽度的不等式关系。

Result: 在多种自然条件下，证明了 subw(H) ∈ Ω(ghw(H) / log ghw(H))，即子模宽度与广义 hypertree 宽度之间存在对数因子的下界关系。

Conclusion: 本文为子模宽度提供了全新的几何视角和工具，不仅给出了可逼近的枝宽等价形式，还揭示了其与经典图论概念的深层联系，为理解合取查询的复杂性结构提供了新途径。

Abstract: Submodular width is a central structural measure governing the complexity of conjunctive query evaluation. In this paper we recast submodular width in geometric terms. We how that submodular width can be approximated, up to a factor $3/2$, by a new branchwidth parameter defined in terms of edge separations in the hypergraph and the costs induced on them by admissible submodular functions. This reformulation turns lower bounds on submodular width into the problem of constructing well-balanced edge separations whose induced cost remains small. We then express this connection through a variational characterisation in terms of a convex body. Using these tools, we relate submodular width to more familiar graph-theoretic notions, including line-graph treewidth and multicommodity flow, and obtain general conditions under which submodular width is tightly linked to generalised hypertree width. In particular, under various natural conditions we show that \[ subw(H) \in Ω\left(\frac{ghw(H)}{\log ghw(H)} \right). \]

</details>


### [17] [Entrywise Low-Rank Approximation and Matrix $p \rightarrow q$ Norms via Global Correlation Rounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22699)
*Prashanti Anderson,Ainesh Bakshi,Samuel Hopkins*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对矩阵逐项低秩近似问题（entrywise low-rank approximation），在偶数 p > 2 且固定秩 k 的情况下，首次给出了多项式时间近似方案（PTAS），并利用 Sherali-Adams 凸层次方法解决了 p > 2 时现有方法（草图和列选择）的瓶颈，同时将同一策略推广到矩阵 p→q 范数的加法近似算法，首次在 p < 2 < q 区域给出了非平凡的加法近似结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于逐项 ℓ_p 范数下的低秩近似问题，当 p = 2 时 SVD 可解，但 p ≠ 2 时计算困难。现有方法在 p > 2 时只能达到常数或双准则近似，缺乏 PTAS。同时，矩阵 p→q 范数在小集扩张和量子信息中有重要应用，p < 2 < q 区域此前缺乏加法近似算法。

Method: 利用 Sherali-Adams 凸层次（凸松弛层次）对优化问题进行建模和求解，通过层次提升逐步逼近原问题，从而绕过草图和列选择方法在 p > 2 时遇到的障碍。

Result: 对于每个固定 k 和偶数 p > 2，给出了首个 PTAS；同时在矩阵 p→q 范数（p < 2 < q）上首次获得非平凡的加法近似算法。

Conclusion: 证明了凸层次方法（Sherali-Adams）可用于设计连续优化问题的 PTAS，为 p > 2 场景下的低秩近似提供了新途径，并展示了该方法在矩阵范数近似中的广泛适用性。

Abstract: Given a matrix $A$, the goal of the entrywise low-rank approximation problem is to find $\operatorname{argmin} \|A-B\|_p$ over all rank-$k$ matrices $B$, where $\| \cdot \|_p$ is the entrywise $\ell_p$ norm. When $p = 2$ this well-studied problem is solved by the singular value decomposition, but for $p \neq 2$ the problem becomes computationally challenging. For every even $p > 2$ and every fixed $k$, we give the first polynomial-time approximation scheme for this problem, improving on the $(3 + \varepsilon)$ approximation of Ban, Bhattiprolu, Bringmann, Kolev, Lee, and Woodruff, the bi-criteria approximation of Woodruff and Yasuda, and the additive approximation scheme of Anderson, Bakshi, and Hopkins. Prior algorithmic approaches based on sketching and column selection, which yielded a polynomial-time approximation scheme in the $p < 2$ setting, face concrete barriers when $p > 2$. Instead, we use the Sherali-Adams hierarchy of convex programs, and in so doing establish a blueprint for how to use convex hierarchies to design polynomial-time approximation schemes for continuous optimization problems.
  We use the same algorithmic strategy to give a new family of additive approximation algorithms for matrix $p \rightarrow q$ norms, which are intimately related to small-set expansion and quantum information. In particular, we give the first nontrivial additive approximation algorithms in the regime $p < 2 < q$.

</details>

### [18] [Feedback Over Form: Why Execution Feedback Matters More Than Pipeline Topology in 1-3B Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21950)
*Charles Junichi McAndrews*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文研究了将1-3B小语言模型组合成代码生成管道的能力。通过执行反馈的自我改进可将代码生成性能提升4个标准差以上，但主要修复运行时错误而非逻辑错误。进化搜索未能发现比简单的"生成-执行-改进"循环更优的管道结构，模型专业化比管道架构更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小语言模型（1-3B）在本地部署方面具有实用性，但在复杂代码生成任务中能力有限。作者探究是否可以通过将多个小模型组合成管道来弥补部分能力损失。

Method: 使用1-3B模型构建代码生成管道，结合执行反馈机制。采用NEAT启发的进化搜索探索不同管道结构（超越简单改进循环）。在HumanEval（164个问题）和sanitized MBPP（427个问题）上进行评估，所有推理均在单台笔记本电脑本地完成。

Result: 自我改进配合执行反馈在两个基准测试上提升超过4个标准差。改进主要修复运行时错误（尤其是NameError和SyntaxError），但很少修复逻辑错误（如AssertionError）。生成器身份不如改进器能力重要：1.5B生成器+3B改进器可匹敌3B模型同时承担两个角色。每次迭代若不设早停则净收益为负。进化搜索基本只发现了同样的简单"生成-执行-改进"循环，未发现更复杂管道带来显著收益。单次评估的适应度会使结果膨胀5-7%。

Conclusion: 在1-3B规模下，执行反馈比管道复杂度对代码生成的提升更重要。模型专业化优于任何通用模型管道配置，进化搜索未发现更优的管道结构。

Abstract: Small language models (1-3B) are practical to run locally, but individually limited on harder code generation tasks. We ask whether composing them into pipelines can recover some of that lost capability. We study code generation pipelines built from 1-3B models with execution feedback, and use a NEAT-inspired evolutionary search to test whether more complex pipeline structure helps beyond a simple refinement loop. We evaluate on HumanEval (164 problems) and sanitized MBPP (427 problems), all with local inference on a single laptop. Self-refinement with execution feedback improves code generation by more than 4 standard deviations on both benchmarks. The gains are narrow in mechanism: refinement fixes many runtime errors (especially NameError and SyntaxError), but rarely fixes logic errors such as AssertionError. Within our tested general-purpose model pool, generator identity mattered less than refiner capability: a 1.5B generator paired with a 3B refiner matched a 3B model doing both roles. Early stopping is essential; without it, every iteration is net-negative. The code-specialized models outperform every general-purpose pipeline configuration, suggesting model specialization matters more than pipeline architecture. Preliminary text-only pipeline experiments without execution feedback did not show gains at this scale. In our constrained search space, evolutionary search mostly rediscovered the same simple generate-execute-refine loop we found manually, with no clearly significant gain from added topology. Single-evaluation fitness inflates results by 5-7 percent, selecting lucky genomes over good ones. On these benchmarks at 1-3B scale, execution feedback mattered more than added pipeline complexity in determining whether composition helped.

</details>

Conclusion: 识别并讨论了三个有前景的研究方向：特定过程组AI代理、基于项目角色的AI代理、以及人类指导的混合协作网络。

Finally, it identifies and discusses three promising research directions for AI-enabled project management, including process group-specific AI agents, project role-based AI agents, and hybrid collaborative networks that enable human-guided orchestration.

### [21] [FlyCatcher: Neural Inference of Runtime Checkers from Tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22028)
*Beatriz Souza,Chang Lou,Suman Nath,Michael Pradel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出 FlyCatcher，一种从现有测试中自动推导运行时检查器的技术，通过结合 LLM 合成、静态分析和动态验证来检测复杂软件系统中的静默故障。在 400 个测试上的评估表明，该方法推断出 334 个检查器，其中 300 个正确，相比现有技术检测到 5.2 倍更多的错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂软件系统常遭受静默故障（即违反预期语义但不引起显式错误），而编写系统特定的运行时检查器虽能有效检测此类错误，但手动编写耗时且具有挑战性，实践中很少进行。

Method: FlyCatcher 结合三种技术从现有测试中自动推导运行时检查器：1) 基于大语言模型的合成，2) 静态分析，3) 动态验证。推导出的检查器是有状态的，通过维护影子状态来抽象实际系统状态，监控特定方法调用并断言应成立的属性。

Result: 在四个广泛使用的复杂软件系统的 400 个测试上评估，FlyCatcher 推断出 334 个检查器，其中 300 个通过交叉验证被认定为正确。相比最先进方法，推断出 2.6 倍更多正确的检查器，检测到 5.2 倍更多错误。

Conclusion: FlyCatcher 通过从测试中自动推断运行时检查器，促进了运行时检查作为检测复杂软件系统中静默故障的实用方法的更广泛采用。

Abstract: Complex software systems often suffer from silent failures, i.e., violations of the intended semantics that do not cause explicit errors. A promising approach to detect such errors is to use system-specific runtime checkers that monitor the execution of a system and check for violations of the intended semantics. However, writing such checkers for a given software system is challenging and time-consuming, and hence, rarely done in practice. This work presents FlyCatcher, an automated approach to derive runtime checkers from existing tests, i.e., from a resource available for most software systems. The critical challenge of such an approach is to generalize the behavioral properties encoded in a test case to arbitrary executions of a system. FlyCatcher addresses this challenge through a combination of LLM-based synthesis, static analysis, and dynamic validation, which infers a checker that monitors specific method calls and asserts properties that should hold when they are called. The inferred checkers are stateful, i.e., they reason about the system's behavior by maintaining a shadow state that abstracts the actual system state as needed by the checker. Our evaluation applies FlyCatcher to 400 tests from four widely used, complex software systems. The approach infers 334 checkers, out of which 300 are found to be correct via cross-validation. Compared with a state-of-the-art approach, our approach infers 2.6x more correct checkers, which enables it to detect 5.2x more errors. By contributing to the automated inference of runtime checkers from tests, this work enables the broader adoption of runtime checking as a practical approach to detect silent failures in complex software systems.

</details>


### [22] [Call-Chain-Aware LLM-Based Test Generation for Java Projects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22046)
*Guancheng Wang,Qinghua Xu,Lionel C. Briand,Zhaoqiang Guo,Kui Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出CAT，一种基于调用链感知的LLM测试生成方法，通过静态分析显式建模调用链和依赖上下文，显著提升单元测试的代码覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的测试生成方法仅依赖执行路径信息构建prompt，对于具有复杂类间依赖、深层调用链和复杂对象初始化需求的软件系统效果不佳。

Method: CAT通过专用静态分析，显式建模调用者-被调用者关系、对象构造函数和第三方依赖，构建可执行的语义有效测试上下文，并支持失败时的迭代测试修复。

Result: 在Defects4J上，CAT相较于SOTA方法PANTA，行覆盖率和分支覆盖率分别提升18.04%和21.74%，并在LLM截止日期后的真实项目上持续取得更优性能。

Conclusion: 调用链和依赖上下文对提升LLM测试生成质量至关重要，CAT通过显式建模这些信息有效解决了现有方法的不足。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have recently shown strong potential for generating project-level unit tests. However, existing state-of-the-art approaches primarily rely on execution-path information to guide prompt construction, which is often insufficient for complex software systems with rich inter-class dependencies, deep call chains, and intricate object initialization requirements. In this paper, we present CAT, a novel call-chain-aware LLM-based test generation approach that explicitly incorporates call-chain and dependency contexts into prompts through dedicated static analysis. To construct executable, semantically valid test contexts, CAT systematically models caller--callee relationships, object constructors, and third-party dependencies, and supports iterative test fixing when generation failures occur. We evaluate CAT on the widely used Defects4J benchmark and on four real-world GitHub projects released after the LLM's cut-off date. The results show that, across projects in Defects4J, CAT improves line and branch coverage by 18.04% and 21.74%, respectively, over the state-of-the-art approach PANTA, while consistently achieving superior performance on post-cutoff real-world projects. An ablation study further demonstrates the importance of call-chain and dependency contexts in CAT.

*Nahian Salsabil,Sebastian Elbaum*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 检索OpenStreetMap数据保留道路拓扑；(2) 利用LLM从道路几何和碰撞前操作推断车辆初始状态；(3) 从半结构化报告生成仿真轨迹。

Result: 生成了52个涵盖多种碰撞类型、道路拓扑和碰撞前操作的多样化事故场景基准。

Conclusion: TRACE提供了首个开源的高保真真实事故仿真资源，为AV系统测试提供了更具挑战性的真实世界失效场景。

Abstract: Validating Autonomous Vehicles (AVs) requires exposure to rare, safety-critical scenarios, infrequent in routine driving data. Existing benchmarks address this by generating synthetic conflicts or mapping accident descriptions to abstract road geometries, failing to capture the topological complexity of real-world crashes. We introduce TRACE , a pipeline that automates the reconstruction of NHTSA crash reports into high-fidelity CARLA simulations by (1) retrieving site-specific OpenStreetMap data to preserve exact road topology, (2) leveraging Large Language Models to infer vehicles' initial state from road geometry and pre-crash maneuvers, and (3) generating simulation trajectories from semi-structured report data. Using this pipeline, we curated a benchmark of 52 diverse accident scenarios covering varied collision types, road topologies, and pre-crash maneuvers, providing a challenging open source resource for testing AV systems against real-world failures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出"伦理测试"概念，区别于现有的公平性测试等方法，专注于检测生成内容中的不道德行为（如有害行为或侵犯知识产权），并通过五个案例研究进行验证。

Abstract: Generative Artificial Intelligence (GAI) systems that can automatically generate content in the form of source code or other contents (e.g., images) has seen increasing popularity due to the emergence of tools such as ChatGPT which rely on Large Language Models (LLMs). Misuse of the automatically generated content can incur serious consequences due to potential harms in the generated content. In this article, we introduce the novel concept of ethics testing which aims to systematically generate tests for identifying software harms. Different from existing testing methodologies (e.g., fairness testing that aims to identifying software discrimination), ethics testing aims to systematically detect software harms that could be induced due to unethical behavior (e.g., harmful behavior or behavior that violates intellectual property rights) in automatically generated content. ### [25] [Evaluating LLM-Based Goal Extraction in Requirements Engineering: Prompting Strategies and Their Limitations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22207)
*Anna Arnaudo,Riccardo Coppola,Maurizio Morisio,Flavio Giobergia,Andrea Bioddo,Angelo Bongiorno,Luca Dadone*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于大语言模型链的自动化目标导向需求工程方法，通过角色识别、高低层目标提取三个阶段，结合上下文学习和生成-批评反馈机制，实现了61%的低层目标识别准确率，适合作为人工提取的加速工具而非完全替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决需求工程中目标导向过程自动化程度不足的问题，利用LLM在文本生成方面的能力，减轻人工提取功能目标的负担。

Method: 构建LLM链（三个LLM串联），分别负责角色识别、高层目标提取和低层目标提取；采用精心设计的提示词；实验多种上下文学习变体；引入生成-批评反馈循环（两个LLM相互校验）；通过消融研究评估各组件贡献。

Result: 低层目标识别准确率为61%；带零样本学习的反馈循环机制优于独立少样本学习；消融实验表明去除反馈循环性能略有下降；但反馈机制与少样本学习结合并未带来优势。

Conclusion: 该管道适合作为加速人工提取的工具，而非完全替代；性能瓶颈可能在于批评LLM的提示策略；未来将引入RAG和CoT提示以提升准确率。

Abstract: Due to the textual and repetitive nature of many Requirements Engineering (RE) artefacts, Large Language Models (LLMs) have proven useful to automate their generation and processing. In this paper, we discuss a possible approach for automating the Goal-Oriented Requirements Engineering (GORE) process by extracting functional goals from software documentation through three phases: actor identification, high and low-level goal extraction. To implement these functionalities, we propose a chain of LLMs fed with engineered prompts. We experimented with different variants of in-context learning and measured the similarities between input data and in-context examples to better investigate their impact. Another key element is the generation-critic mechanism, implemented as a feedback loop involving two LLMs. Although the pipeline achieved 61% accuracy in low-level goal identification, the final stage, these results indicate the approach is best suited as a tool to accelerate manual extraction rather than as a full replacement. The feedback-loop mechanism with Zero-shot outperformed stand-alone Few-shot, with an ablation study suggesting that performance slightly degrades without the feedback cycle. However, we reported that the combination of the feedback mechanism with Few-shot does not deliver any advantage, possibly suggesting that the primary performance ceiling is the prompting strategy applied to the 'critic' LLM. Together with the refinement of both the quantity and quality of the Shot examples, future research will integrate Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) and Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting to improve accuracy.

### [26] [RAG-Reflect: Agentic Retrieval-Augmented Generation with Reflections for Comment-Driven Code Maintenance on Stack Overflow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22217)
*Mehedi Hasan Shanto,Muhammad Asaduzzaman,Alioune Ngom*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出RAG-Reflect框架，结合检索增强推理与自我反思机制，在不需任务特定训练的情况下，在Stack Overflow评论-代码编辑验证任务上达到接近微调模型的性能（F1=0.78）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线编程平台（如Stack Overflow）上大量用户评论仅为表达感谢或澄清，只有少数评论能触发有意义的代码编辑。现有方法难以有效识别那些真正驱动代码修改的"有效评论"，需要一种无需额外训练数据就能准确判断评论-编辑因果关系的方法。

Method: RAG-Reflect框架包含三个阶段运行流程：(1) 初始化阶段，通过Interpretation模块分析知识库生成验证规则；(2) 推理阶段，依次进行上下文示例检索、评论-编辑因果关系推理、基于预置规则的自我反思决策。整体采用模块化设计，集成大语言模型与检索增强生成技术。

Result: 在SOUP基准测试上，RAG-Reflect达到Precision=0.81、Recall=0.74、F1=0.78，优于Logistic Regression、XGBoost等传统基线及多种提示工程技术，且接近微调模型性能（F1=0.773），而无需重新训练。消融实验表明检索和反思模块均显著提升性能。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过检索增强推理与自我反思机制的模块化组合，可以在无需任务特定训练的情况下达到接近微调模型的性能，为软件维护任务中应用智能体AI原则提供了有效范例。

Abstract: User comments on online programming platforms such as Stack Overflow play a vital role in maintaining the correctness and relevance of shared code examples. However, the majority of comments express gratitude or clarification, while only a small fraction highlight actionable issues that drive meaningful edits. This paper demonstrates how agentic AI principles can revolutionize software maintenance tasks by presenting RAG-Reflect, a modular framework that achieves fine-tuned-level performance for valid comment-edit prediction without task-specific training. Valid Comment-Edit Prediction (VCP) is the task of determining whether a user comment directly triggered a subsequent code edit. The framework integrates large language models (LLMs) with retrieval-augmented reasoning and self-reflection mechanisms. RAG-Reflect operates through a three-stage runtime workflow built on a one-time pattern analysis phase. During initialization, an Interpretation module analyzes the knowledge base to generate validation rules. At inference time, the system (1) retrieves contextual examples, (2) reasons about comment-edit causality, and (3) reflects on decisions using the pre-established rules. We evaluate RAG-Reflect on the publicly available SOUP benchmark, achieving Precision = 0.81, Recall = 0.74, and F1 = 0.78, outperforming traditional baselines (e.g., Logistic Regression, XGBoost, different prompting techniques) and closely approaching the performance of fine-tuned models (F1 = 0.773) without retraining. Our ablation and stage-level analyses show that both retrieval and reflection modules substantially enhance performance.

</details>

### [28] [R2Code: A Self-Reflective LLM Framework for Requirements-to-Code Traceability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22432)
*Yifei Wang,Jacky Keung,Xiaoxue Ma,Zhenyu Mao,Kehui Chen,Yishu Li*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: R2Code是一个基于LLM的语义追溯框架，通过双向对齐网络、自反思一致性验证和动态上下文自适应检索三个组件，在需求-代码追溯中平均F1提升7.4%，同时降低41.7%的token消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于IR和embedding的需求-代码追溯方法过度依赖词汇相似度，跨项目跨语言时链接不完整或不一致，且长上下文检索和提示带来高成本。

Method: R2Code包含三个组件：1) 分解增强的双向对齐网络(BAN)，对齐四层需求语义与代码结构；2) 自反思一致性验证(SRCV)，通过解释引导的一致性检查校准链接可靠性；3) 动态上下文自适应检索(DCAR)，基于语义重叠权重调整检索粒度并过滤上下文。

Result: 在五个跨领域、跨编程语言的公开数据集上，R2Code平均F1值提升7.4%，通过自适应上下文控制token消耗减少高达41.7%。

Conclusion: R2Code通过语义对齐、一致性验证和自适应检索，有效提升了需求-代码追溯的准确性和效率，显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Accurate requirement-to-code traceability is crucial for software maintenance. However, existing IR- and embedding-based methods are heavily dependent on lexical similarity, often yielding incomplete or inconsistent links across projects and languages and incurring high cost from long-context retrieval and prompting. This paper presents R2Code, an LLM-based semantic traceability framework designed to improve trace link accuracy while reducing inference cost. R2Code integrates three components: 1) a decomposition-enhanced Bidirectional Alignment Network (BAN) that aligns four-layer requirement semantics with corresponding code structures to support cross-level semantic matching; 2) a Self-Reflective Consistency Verification (SRCV) module that conducts explanation-guided consistency checking to calibrate link reliability; and 3) a Dynamic Context-Adaptive Retrieval (DCAR) mechanism that adjusts retrieval granularity and filters contexts using semantic-overlap weighting for efficient context utilization. Experiments on five public datasets spanning multiple domains and two programming languages demonstrate that R2Code consistently outperforms the strongest baselines, achieving an average F1 gain of 7.4%, while reducing token consumption by up to 41.7% through adaptive context control.

### [32] [From Natural Language to Verified Code: Toward AI Assisted Problem-to-Code Generation with Dafny-Based Formal Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22601)

Method: 构建NL2VC-60数据集（60个复杂算法问题），评估7个开源LLM在11个随机子集上的表现。采用三级提示策略：1) 无上下文提示；2) 签名提示（提供结构锚点）；3) 自愈提示（利用Dafny验证器迭代反馈）。同时集成uDebug平台进行功能验证，防止空洞验证（即用平凡规约欺骗验证器）。

Result: 无上下文提示几乎全部失败；签名提示和自愈提示显著提升性能。Gemma 4-31B验证成功率达90.91%，GPT-OSS 120B从0%提升至81.82%。结果表明开源LLM通过适当引导可实现有效的形式化验证代码合成。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise in automated software engineering, yet their guarantee of correctness is frequently undermined by erroneous or hallucinated code. To enforce model honesty, formal verification requires LLMs to synthesize implementation logic alongside formal specifications that are subsequently proven correct by a mathematical verifier. However, the transition from informal natural language to precise formal specification remains an arduous task. Our work addresses this by providing the NaturalLanguage2VerifiedCode (NL2VC)-60 dataset: a collection of 60 complex algorithmic problems. We evaluate 11 randomly selected problem sets across seven open-weight LLMs using a tiered prompting strategy: contextless prompts, signature prompts providing structural anchors, and self-healing prompts utilizing iterative feedback from the Dafny verifier. To address vacuous verification, where models satisfy verifiers with trivial specifications, we integrate the uDebug platform to ensure functional validation. Our results show that while contextless prompting leads to near-universal failure, structural signatures and iterative self-healing facilitate a dramatic performance turnaround. Specifically, Gemma 4-31B achieved a 90.91\% verification success rate, while GPT-OSS 120B rose from zero to 81.82\% success with signature-guided feedback. These findings indicate that formal verification is now attainable for open-weight LLMs, which serve as effective apprentices for synthesizing complex annotations and facilitating high-assurance software development.

### [33] [Quality-Driven Selective Mutation for Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22640)
*Zaheed Ahmed,Emmanuel Charleson Dapaah,Philip Makedonski,Jens Grabowski*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习突变测试文献缺乏一个统一的度量标准来同时衡量突变体的抵抗性和真实性，导致难以高效筛选高质量的突变算子配置以降低成本。

Method: 提出一个概率框架，通过统计杀死概率衡量抵抗性（适应经典难杀死突变概念），通过广义Jaccard相似度衡量真实性（比较突变体与真实缺陷的可检测模式），从而对突变算子配置进行排序和过滤。

Result: 在四个真实深度学习缺陷数据集上评估，其中三个用于估计和选择高质量算子配置，一个用于验证。结果表明，质量驱动选择可在保持抵抗性和真实性典型水平的前提下，减少高达55.6%的突变体生成数量。

Conclusion: 双目标选择能够在降低成本的同时，不损害突变体在测试目标或真实缺陷模拟任一角色中的实用性。

Abstract: Mutants support testing and debugging in two roles: (i) as test goals and (ii) as substitutes for real faults. Hard-to-kill mutants provide better guidance for test improvement, while realism is essential when mutants are used to simulate real bugs. Building on these roles, selective mutation for deep learning (DL) aims to reduce the cost of mutant generation and execution by choosing operator configurations that yield resistant and realistic mutants. However, the DL literature lacks a unified measure that captures both aspects. This study presents a probabilistic framework to quantify mutant quality along two complementary axes: resistance and realism. Resistance adapts the classical notion of hard-to-kill mutants to the DL setting using statistical killing probabilities, while realism is measured via the generalized Jaccard similarity between mutant and real-fault detectability patterns. The framework enables ranking and filtering of low-quality mutation-operator configurations without assuming a specific use case. We empirically evaluate the approach on four datasets of real DL faults. Three datasets (CleanML, DeepFD, and DeepLocalize) are used to estimate and select high-quality operator configurations, and the held-out defect4ML dataset is used for validation. Results show that quality-driven selection reduces the number of generated mutants by up to 55.6% while preserving typical levels of resistance and realism under baseline-aligned selection thresholds. These findings confirm that dual-objective selection can lower cost without compromising the usefulness of mutants for either role.

A recent meta-analysis study found empirical support for this hypothesis: a small correlation between the sum of verifier warnings and human-derived code comprehensibility metrics. Based on this finding, we conjectured that using the sum of verifier tool (verifier) warnings to represent program semantic information as an input feature to machine learning (ML) models for code comprehensibility prediction can enhance their performance, when combined with traditional syntactic and developer features.

Our findings suggest that while a correlation exists, the verifier warning sum offers limited discriminative power: combining syntactic and developer features is just as effective for predicting human-judged code comprehensibility.

Motivation: 现有代码生成基准（如HumanEval）使用自然语言需求进行评估，但实际企业开发中开发者通常基于结构化设计（如UML图）编写代码，导致现有基准无法真实反映LLMs在真实软件工程中的代码生成能力。

Method: 提出RealBench基准，包含自然语言需求+UML系统设计的仓库级代码生成任务，并对多个先进LLMs进行系统评估，分析不同生成策略（一次性生成、逐模块生成等）的效果。

Result: 1) LLMs在仓库级代码生成上表现明显更差，且模型间性能差距显著；2) LLMs能较好识别UML中的模块，但生成质量因语法和逻辑错误而较差；3) 小仓库适合一次性全部生成，复杂仓库适合逐模块生成策略。

Conclusion: 现有基准高估了LLMs在实际企业开发中的代码生成能力，RealBench能更真实地反映其水平，并揭示了当前LLMs在仓库级结构化代码生成中的关键局限性。

Abstract: Writing code requires significant time and effort in software development. To automate this process, researchers have made substantial progress using Large Language Models (LLMs) for code generation. Many benchmarks like HumanEval and EvoCodeBench have been created to evaluate LLMs by requiring them to generate code from natural language requirements. However, in enterprise applications and team development, developers typically write code based on structured designs or specifications rather than raw natural language descriptions. This gap between existing benchmarks and real industry development practices means that current benchmark scores may not accurately reflect how much code generation can help automate software development tasks.
  To address this gap, we propose RealBench, a repository-level code generation benchmark aligned with real-world industry software development practices. Each example includes both natural language requirements and UML diagrams as system design, matching how developers typically receive specifications. Based on the constructed benchmarks, we conduct a systematic evaluation of advanced LLMs' code generation capabilities when provided with structured system designs. The experimental results reveal key insights in current LLMs' capabilities for repo-level code generation aligned with real-world software development practices. First, we notice that regarding repo-level code generation, LLMs show much worse performance and there are significant performance gaps among LLMs. Second, LLMs are good at finding and creating modules defined in UML diagrams, but the quality of generated modules is often poor due to grammar and logic errors. Third, generating the entire repository at once is the best generation strategy on smaller repositories, while generating a complex repository with the module-by-module strategy works better compared to other strategies.

</details>


### [36] [Inferring Equivalence Classes from Legacy Undocumented Embedded Binaries for ISO 26262-Compliant Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22673)
*Marco De Luca,Domenico Francesco De Angelis,Domenico Amalfitano,Pasquale Cimmino,Anna Rita Fasolino*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在二进制级别直接从编译固件中推断面向输出的等价类的方法，无需依赖源代码注释或外部文档。该方法结合控制流重建和引导符号执行，分析单个函数并根据不可区分的可观察行为（包括返回值和输出参数）对执行路径进行分组。在工业汽车环境中的实践者研究表明，该方法与专家期望高度一致，具有良好的可读性和实用性，能够支持对遗留无文档安全嵌入式软件的系统测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在工业实践中，等价类划分这一安全标准（如ISO 26262）要求的测试设计技术，往往因遗留无文档嵌入式固件的功能规格说明不完整或过时而难以应用。现有方法依赖源代码级别的注释或外部文档，不适用于仅有编译后二进制固件的场景。

Method: 提出二进制级别的等价类推断方法：(1) 控制流重建，(2) 引导符号执行分析单个函数，(3) 根据不可区分的可观察行为（返回值、输出参数）对执行路径分组，(4) 可选的后处理步骤生成人类可读表示。

Result: 在工业汽车环境中通过实践者研究进行评估，结果表明该方法与专家期望高度一致，并且在可读性和实用性方面获得积极评价，能够支持函数理解和测试设计。

Conclusion: 证明了二进制级别等价类推断在遗留无文档安全嵌入式软件系统测试中的可行性和实际相关性，为工业实践提供了一种无需文档即可进行等价类划分的有效途径。

Abstract: Equivalence class partitioning is a well-established test design technique mandated by safety standards such as ISO~26262 for systematic testing of safety software. In industrial practice, however, its application to legacy undocumented embedded firmware is often hindered by incomplete or outdated functional specifications.
  This paper proposes a binary-level methodology for inferring output-oriented equivalence classes directly from compiled firmware, without relying on source-level annotations or external documentation. The approach combines control-flow reconstruction and guided symbolic execution to analyze individual functions and group execution paths according to indistinguishable observable behavior, including return values and output parameters. An optional post-processing step produces human-readable representations to support comprehension and documentation.
  The methodology is evaluated in an industrial automotive context through a practitioner-based study assessing correctness and interpretability. Results indicate strong alignment with expert expectations and a positive perception of readability and usefulness for supporting function understanding and test design. These findings demonstrate the feasibility and practical relevance of binary-level equivalence class inference for systematic testing of legacy undocumented safety-embedded software.

### [37] [Code for All: Educational Applications of the "Vibe Coding" Hackathon in Programming Education across All Skill Levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22747)
*Ashley J. Chen,Yijia Cao,Minghao Shao,Ramesh Karri,Muhammad Shafique*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过为期一个月的在线黑客松，研究了"氛围编程"（vibe coding）在编程教育中的价值。参与者从新手到专家，仅使用LLM生成代码（无手动编辑），完成从基础前端到生产级应用的不同难度项目。混合方法评估显示，这种AI辅助编程方式在不同背景参与者中展现出不同的学习和实践模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 为期一个月的线上黑客松，面向多国参与者（从新手到专家），设置三个递增难度赛道（Spark基础前端、Build后端/数据库集成、Launch生产级应用）。参与者仅使用LLM生成代码，不能手动编辑，需提交完整聊天记录、源码、演示视频和功能报告。采用混合方法评估：标准化项目评分（功能、UI/UX、影响力、提示质量、代码可读性）+ 赛后调查（感知学习成果）+ 开放式反馈主题分析。

Result: 揭示了不同背景参与者随任务复杂度增加如何参与氛围编程；"无手动编辑"约束如何塑造提示和调试实践；以及这些模式对将AI辅助开发融入编程教育和竞争性学习环境的意义。

Conclusion: 氛围编程在编程教育中有潜在价值，但其效果因参与者背景和任务复杂度而异。"无手动编辑"的约束改变了传统的编程调试流程，提示质量成为关键技能。这些发现对如何将AI辅助编程整合到教育环境中提供了重要启示。

Abstract: The emergence of large language models has enabled vibe coding, a natural language approach to programming in which users describe intent and AI generates or revises code, potentially broadening access to programming while preserving meaningful learning outcomes. We investigate its educational value through a month-long online hackathon that welcomed participants from multiple countries, ranging from complete beginners to experienced developers. The hackathon offered three tracks with increasing technical demands. Spark emphasized basic frontend functionality and dynamic features such as buttons, forms, and API calls. Build required backend or database integration. Launch targeted production ready web applications, including deployment. Participants were required to develop projects using only LLM generated code without manual edits and submitted complete chat histories, source code, demo videos, and functionality reports. We assessed educational effectiveness with a mixed methods design that combined standardized project evaluations across functionality, user interface and user experience design, impact, prompt quality, and code readability, along with post-hackathon surveys of perceived learning outcomes and thematic analysis of open-ended feedback. Our findings describe how participants with different backgrounds engage with vibe coding as task complexity increases, how the no manual editing constraint shapes prompting and debugging practices, and what these patterns imply for integrating AI assisted development into programming education and competitive learning environments.

### [38] [OCC: Physical-Layer Assisted Congestion Control for Real-Time Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22383)
*Yufan Zhuang,Zili Meng,Zehong Lin,Jun Zhang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 针对6G实时通信中低延迟与高吞吐难以兼得的问题，本文提出OCC方案，利用物理层信息实时获取可用带宽，通过帧感知测量、应用限制感知估计和编码器友好速率控制三大策略，在真实蜂窝测试中将尾延迟降低13%-68%，视频码率提升1.2-3.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RTC方案依赖试错机制，无法快速准确地探测可用带宽，导致延迟可靠性与带宽利用率之间存在根本性矛盾。随着蜂窝网络带宽和应用需求波动范围增大，这一矛盾变得尤为严峻。

Method: 利用物理层信息实时获取可用带宽，并提出三项创新策略：(1) 帧感知带宽测量，应对流量突发；(2) 应用限制感知带宽估计，应对APP限制；(3) 编码器友好速率控制，应对编码器滞后问题。

Result: 在开源蜂窝测试平台上进行的真实空口实验表明，OCC显著提升了移动RTC性能，尾网络延迟降低13%至68%，视频帧码率提升1.2倍至3.5倍。

Conclusion: OCC通过利用物理层信息实现了对动态无线网络条件的快速自适应，有效打破了延迟与带宽利用率之间的权衡，为6G实时通信提供了一种可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Real-time communications (RTC) is a core technology for emerging applications in 6G, such as cloud gaming, teleoperation, and extended reality (XR), which require consistently low latency and high bitrates. Existing RTC solutions fundamentally struggle to maintain low latency while supporting high bitrates due to their reliance on trial-and-error-based mechanisms. These mechanisms fail to probe the available bandwidth (ABW) promptly and accurately, leading to a trade-off between latency reliability and bandwidth utilization. The tension becomes extremely more critical as the cellular bandwidth and application's demand fluctuate with a larger range in cellular networks nowadays. To address this trade-off, we propose OCC, a novel approach that utilizes physical-layer information to explicitly obtain the ABW in real time, enabling rapid adaptation to dynamic wireless network conditions. However, the unique characteristics of RTC, including traffic bursts, application (APP) limits, and encoder lag, make the physical-layer informed control non-trivial. OCC effectively addresses these issues through three innovative strategies: frame-aware bandwidth measurement, APP-limit-aware bandwidth estimation, and encoder-friendly rate control. Extensive over-the-air experiments on an open-source cellular testbed demonstrate that OCC significantly enhances the performance of mobile RTC, reducing tail network latency by $13\%$ to $68\%$ and improving video frame bitrate by $1.2\times$ to $3.5\times$.

</details>


### [39] [Benchmarking LLM-Driven Network Configuration Repair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22513)
*Ioannis Protogeros,Rufat Asadli,Benjamin Hoffman,Laurent Vanbever*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出 Cornetto，首个用于评估 LLM 在网络配置修复任务中功能正确性与可扩展性的基准。通过形式化验证和多样化场景合成，测试了 9 个 SOTA 模型，发现 LLM 虽有潜力但常引入回归问题，性能随规模下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法评估 LLM 能否在不引入新故障的情况下修复大规模、相互依赖的网络配置错误，亟需一个场景多样、复杂度递增且评估方式明确可靠的基准。

Method: 构建了一个生成管线，合成代表性且合理的错误配置场景；并采用形式化验证框架，根据真实规范评估修复方案的功能正确性。最终合成了包含 231 个问题的数据集，覆盖不同拓扑规模（20-754 节点）和多种协议。

Result: 评估了 9 个 SOTA LLM，发现它们虽有潜力，但常引入回归（新故障），且性能随网络规模增大而显著下降。

Conclusion: 可靠的 LLM 驱动的网络自动化需要将 LLM 与形式化验证引导的迭代工作流相结合，而非单纯依赖一次性修复。

Abstract: There is a rapidly growing interest in using Large Language Models (LLMs) to automate complex network operations, but their reliable adoption requires rigorous assessment of their effectiveness and safety. Existing benchmarks do not address whether LLMs can successfully resolve errors in large-scale, interdependent network configurations without introducing new disruptions. Developing such a benchmark is challenging: scenarios must be diverse and increasingly complex, yet their evaluation must be straightforward and meaningful. In this paper, we present Cornetto, the first benchmark to evaluate LLM-driven network configuration repair functionally and at scale. Cornetto features a generation pipeline that synthesizes representative and plausible misconfiguration scenarios, coupled with an evaluation framework that uses formal verification to assess functional correctness of proposed fixes against ground-truth specifications. Using this pipeline, we synthesize a dataset of 231 problems for fixing configurations across varying network topologies (20--754 nodes) and diverse protocols. We evaluate 9 state-of-the-art LLMs and find that while they show promise, they often introduce regressions and their performance degrades at scale. Our results indicate that reliable LLM-powered network automation requires integrating LLMs into iterative workflows guided by formal verification.

</details>


### [40] [Chamelio: A Fast Shared Cloud Network Stack for Isolated Tenant-Defined Protocols](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22603)
*Matheus Stolet,Simon Peter,Antoine Kaufmann*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: Chamelio是一个可编程的共享网络栈，通过有界eBPF快速路径和租户慢速路径，让租户实现完整协议，同时保持固定共享栈的性能和强隔离性。它结合共享栈架构、联合优化和有界快速路径合约与运行时周期计数三大技术，在TCP场景下达到9.2 Mreq/s，将可编程开销从23.9%降至3.8%，并将受害尾延迟从154微秒降至46微秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统云网络虚拟化存在CPU成本高和尾延迟膨胀的问题，而共享主机数据路径虽然通过跨租户的统一优化路径解决了这些问题，但其固定功能特性使租户无法定制协议。eBPF虽然可以恢复可编程性，但现有扩展粒度太小，且验证器只提供安全保证而非性能隔离——一个租户的每包计算会膨胀其他租户的尾延迟。

Method: Chamelio提出三项关键技术：1) 共享栈架构，允许租户定义协议；2) 联合优化，在共享快速路径中将租户处理程序与提供商基础设施及共存租户联合编译优化；3) 有界快速路径合约与运行时周期计数，在保持可编程性的同时实现强性能隔离。

Result: 租户可编程TCP达到9.2 Mreq/s，与手工调优的TAS栈持平；联合编译将可编程税从23.9%降至3.8%；在TCP扩展攻击下，未受保护的栈的尾延迟膨胀至154微秒，而Chamelio将受害者的尾延迟控制在46微秒。

Conclusion: Chamelio证明了在共享网络栈中同时实现租户协议可编程性和强性能隔离是可行的，其有界快速路径合约和运行时周期计数为未来云网络的可编程基础设施提供了重要设计思路。

Abstract: Conventional cloud network virtualization sends packets through multiple guest and host layers, inflating CPU cost and tail latency. Shared host datapaths collapse this layering into one optimized path across tenants, but existing shared stacks are fixed-function: tenants cannot specialize their protocols. eBPF is the natural vehicle for restoring programmability to a shared datapath, but today's extensions are hook-sized, and its verifier provides safety -- not performance isolation: one tenant's per-packet work can inflate every other tenant's tail latency.
  Chamelio is a programmable shared network stack that lets tenants implement full protocols through a bounded eBPF fast path and a tenant slow path, while approaching the performance and preserving the strong isolation of fixed shared stacks. It combines three ideas: a shared-stack architecture for tenant-defined protocols; joint optimisation of tenant handlers with provider infrastructure and co-resident tenants in the shared fast path; and a bounded fast path contract with runtime cycle accounting that keeps tenant programmability compatible with strong performance isolation. A tenant programmable TCP on Chamelio reaches 9.2 Mreq/s, matching the hand-tuned TAS stack; joint compilation shrinks the programmability tax from 23.9% to 3.8%; and under a scaling TCP adversary that drives uninstrumented stacks to 154 microseconds, Chamelio bounds victim tail latency at 46 microseconds.

</details>


### [41] [Evaluation of the effects of 3GPP-specific beamforming and channel estimation on the 3D EIRP profile of a 5G gNB](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22710)
*Armed Tusha,Joshua Roy Palathinkal,Monisha Ghosh*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文首次基于3GPP Release-18标准，评估了5G NR基站（gNB）在FR-1频段的三维EIRP特征，揭示了现有码本设计在抑制对雷达/卫星等现有服务干扰方面的不足。研究发现：旁瓣导致干扰不限于最差波束方向；天线架构影响三维EIRP；提出的两种波束归零方法虽能实现11 dB定向功率降低，但导致UE链路SNR损失3.5-4.5 dB（在10^{-4} BER下），高于理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 5G NR利用三维波束成形和中频段频谱（如4.4-4.9 GHz和7.125-7.4 GHz）提升性能，但高定向传输可能对雷达和卫星等现有服务造成干扰。现有研究多采用简化的理论分析（如波束归零），缺乏基于实际3GPP标准的三维EIRP评估，因此需要更真实的量化分析。

Method: 基于3GPP Release-18 FR-1标准，对gNB的三维EIRP进行实测/仿真评估；分析不同码本设计、AAS架构和天线端口配置下的三维EIRP特征；提出两种波束归零方法，并在理想和实际信道估计下测试其对UE链路性能的影响（以10^{-4} BER为基准）。

Result: 1) gNB的干扰不仅来自最差波束方向，旁瓣贡献显著；2) AAS架构和天线端口配置对平均三维EIRP有重要影响；3) 提出的波束归零方法可实现11 dB定向功率降低，但导致UE链路SNR损失3.5-4.5 dB（10^{-4} BER下），高于理论分析预测。

Conclusion: 现有3GPP码本设计在三维空间EIRP控制上存在问题，实际波束归零的SNR代价高于理论预期，需要在干扰抑制和UE性能之间进一步权衡。研究为5G NR与现有中频段服务共存提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Spatial domain exploitation through 3D beamforming serves as a critical technology enabler for performance enhancement in the Fifth Generation New Radio (5G NR) specification. This is realized at the gNodeB (gNB) through the integration of massive antenna element arrays that facilitates 3D spatial multiplexing. However, these systems with high-directional transmissions also represent a threat to incumbent services such as radar and satellites. These incumbents already operate in midband spectrum\textemdash{}including the 4.4-4.9 GHz and 7.125-7.4 GHz bands\textemdash{}that are currently being evaluated for future cellular deployments. Here, we present the first work that evaluates the transmitted Effective Isotropic Radiated Power (EIRP) of a gNB in 3D space, using the 3GPP Release-18 standard for FR-1 instead of theoretical analyses of beam nulling, which can be simplistic. We shed light on the problems requiring attention with the EIRP profile in 3D space for existing codebook designs predefined in 3GPP: i) interference from a gNB does not depend only on the worst-case beamforming direction, but on a variety of beamforming directions due to side-lobes; ii) advanced antenna systems (AAS) architecture and antenna port configurations play a crucial role in average 3D EIRP, which are implementation dependent, and iii) we introduce two beam nulling methods, which achieve a 11 dB power reduction toward a target direction, with 3.5-4.5 dB SNR loss in UE link performance at a 10^{-4} bit error rate (BER) across modulation schemes under ideal and practical channel estimation, a higher loss compared to predictions from theoretical analyses.

</details>

### [42] [Focus Session: Hardware and Software Techniques for Accelerating Multimodal Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21952)
*Muhammad Shafique,Abdul Basit,Muhammad Abdullah Hanif,Alberto Marchisio,Rachmad Vidya Wicaksana Putra,Minghao Shao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多层方法论，通过硬件软件协同设计、模型压缩（混合精度量化、结构化剪枝）、推理优化（推测解码、模型级联）以及专用硬件加速器，高效加速多模态基础模型（MFMs），并在医疗和代码生成任务上验证了有效性，最后扩展到节能脉冲MFMs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态基础模型（MFMs）计算和内存需求巨大，现有加速方法不够系统化，缺乏从硬件到软件的全面协同优化方案。

Method: ①硬件-软件协同设计transformer模块；②模型压缩：层次感知混合精度量化+结构化剪枝；③推理优化：推测解码、小到大模型级联（轻量自测试决定何时升级）、序列长度/视觉分辨率/步长协同优化、图级算子融合；④专用硬件加速器（专家设计或LLM辅助设计）；⑤基于硬件架构优化处理数据流和内存高效注意力机制。

Result: 在医疗多模态任务和代码生成任务上验证了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本方法论能有效加速多模态基础模型，并具有向节能脉冲MFMs扩展的潜力。

Abstract: This work presents a multi-layered methodology for efficiently accelerating multimodal foundation models (MFMs). It combines hardware and software co-design of transformer blocks with an optimization pipeline that reduces computational and memory requirements. During model development, it employs performance enhancements through fine-tuning for domain-specific adaptation. Our methodology further incorporates hardware and software techniques for optimizing MFMs. Specifically, it employs MFM compression using hierarchy-aware mixed-precision quantization and structural pruning for transformer blocks and MLP channels. It also optimizes operations through speculative decoding, model cascading that routes queries through a small-to-large cascade and uses lightweight self-tests to determine when to escalate to larger models, as well as co-optimization of sequence length, visual resolution & stride, and graph-level operator fusion. To efficiently execute the model, the processing dataflow is optimized based on the underlying hardware architecture together with memory-efficient attention to meet on-chip bandwidth and latency budgets. To support this, a specialized hardware accelerator for the transformer workloads is employed, which can be developed through expert design or an LLM-aided design approach. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed methodology on medical-MFMs and on code generation tasks, and conclude with extensions toward energy-efficient spiking-MFMs.

</details>

We evaluate two learning formulations: indirect heatmap-based models that predict received-power radio maps, and direct score-map models that predict the objective landscape over feasible transmitter locations. Within the heatmap family, discriminative models deliver one-shot predictions 1350-2400x faster than exhaustive search, while diffusion models additionally support multi-sample inference that improves single-objective performance and, by reusing the same sample pool under a balanced criterion, recovers strong balanced placements without explicit multi-objective training. Dual score-map strategies combining power and coverage score maps match the exhaustive balanced optimum ($\bar{d}=2.60$) and remain close across smaller candidate budgets, at 14-22x speedups after candidate re-evaluation. Both formulations admit very fast one-shot inference; on this benchmark, dual score-map methods are strongest for balanced placement, whereas heatmap formulations remain attractive for their physically meaningful intermediate maps and, in the diffusion setting, for inference-time search.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大规模多任务优化方法（如MAP-Elites变体）依赖于固定的离散化存档，忽略了任务空间的拓扑结构，且基于种群的方法难以扩展到大量任务。

Method: 将任务空间建模为图（任务为节点，任务参数空间的连接为边），融合社交学习（邻居节点间的交叉操作）与个体学习（节点独立变异）两种机制进行知识迁移和优化。

Abstract: Multi-task optimization is a powerful approach for solving a large number of tasks in parallel. However, existing algorithms face distinct limitations: Population-based methods scale poorly and remain underexplored for large task sets. Approaches that do scale beyond a thousand tasks are mostly MAP-Elites variants and rely on a fixed, discretized archive that disregards the topology of the task space. We introduce MONET (Multi-Task Optimization over Networks of Tasks), a multi-task optimization algorithm that models the task space as a graph: tasks are nodes, and edges connect tasks in the task parameter space. This representation enables knowledge transfer between tasks and remains tractable for high-dimensional problems while exploiting the topology of the task space. MONET combines social learning, which generates candidates from neighboring nodes via crossover, with individual learning, which refines a node's own solution independently via mutation. We evaluate MONET on four domains (archery, arm, and cartpole with 5,000 tasks each; hexapod with 2,000 tasks) and show that it matches or exceeds the performance of existing MAP-Elites-based baselines across all four domains.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 记忆令牌不可或缺；最佳数量为8-32个（57.4%精确匹配）；ACT比固定深度更稳定（56.9% vs 53.4%）；λ预热可减少34%的ponder步骤，精度相当（57.0%）；注意力头分化为记忆读取器、约束传播器和集成器。
