Abstract: Shapley values are a cornerstone of explainable AI, yet their proliferation into competing formulations has created a fragmented landscape with little consensus on practical deployment. While theoretical differences are well-documented, evaluation remains reliant on quantitative proxies whose alignment with human utility is unverified. In this work, we use a unified amortized framework to isolate semantic differences between eight Shapley variants under the low-latency constraints of operational risk workflows. We conduct a large-scale empirical evaluation across four risk datasets and a realistic fraud-detection environment involving professional analysts and 3,735 case reviews. Our results reveal a fundamental misalignment: standard quantitative metrics, such as sparsity and faithfulness, are decoupled from human-perceived clarity and decision utility. Furthermore, while no formulation improved objective analyst performance, explanations consistently increased decision confidence, signaling a critical risk of automation bias in high-stakes settings. These findings suggest that current evaluation proxies are insufficient for predicting downstream human impact, and we provide evidence-based guidance for selecting formulations and metrics in operational decision systems.

### [97] [Iterative Model-Learning Scheme via Gaussian Processes for Nonlinear Model Predictive Control of (Semi-)Batch Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22672)
*Tai Xuan Tan,Alexander Mitsos,Eike Cramer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于高斯过程（GP）的模型学习非线性模型预测控制（GP-MLMPC）方案，用于批次过程。该方法仅需一条初始轨迹数据即可启动，通过迭代运行批次并更新GP模型，在数次迭代后性能可达到与全模型NMPC媲美的水平。在半间歇聚合反应器仿真中，跟踪误差降低83%，经济目标下最终产品质量提升17倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 批次过程具有固有的瞬态特性和非线性，适合采用非线性模型预测控制（NMPC），但NMPC的应用受限于动态模型的高成本和难以获取。因此，作者希望提出一种无需精确机理模型、仅依赖数据驱动的方法来实现NMPC控制。

Method: 提出GP-MLMPC方案：使用单条初始轨迹（如PI控制器生成的数据）初始化GP模型；迭代运行NMPC（嵌入GP模型）控制批次过程，每轮迭代后用新观测数据更新GP模型；利用GP的不确定性量化构建机会约束，确保操作安全并满足置信水平要求。

Result: 在半间歇聚合反应器仿真中，跟踪任务下经过4次迭代，跟踪误差相比初始轨迹降低83%；经济任务下经过8次迭代，最终产品质量提升17倍。两种任务下性能均与全模型NMPC相当。

Conclusion: GP-MLMPC方案是一种数据高效、无需机理知识的批次过程控制方法，能够通过迭代学习逼近最优控制器，在安全约束下实现快速收敛，具有较好的应用前景。

Abstract: Batch processes are inherently transient and typically nonlinear, motivating nonlinear model predictive control (NMPC). However, adopting NMPC is hindered by the cost and unavailability of dynamic models. Thus, we propose to use Gaussian Processes (GP) in a model-learning NMPC scheme (GP-MLMPC) for batch processes. We initialize the GP-MLMPC using data from a single initial trajectory, e.g., from a PI controller. We iteratively apply the NMPC embedded with GPs to run batches and update the GP with new observations from each iteration, thereby achieving batch-wise improvements. Using uncertainty quantification from the GPs, we formulate chance constraints to enforce safe operation to the required confidence levels. We demonstrate our approach in \textit{silico} on a semi-batch polymerization reactor for tracking and economic objectives over durations of two hours, and the reactor temperature is constrained in a range of $\pm2^\circ C$ around its setpoint. After only four batch iterations, tracking error from the GP-MLMPC scheme converged to a reduction of $83\%$, compared to the initial trajectory. Furthermore, under an economic objective, the GP-MLMPC resulted in a 17-fold increase in final product mass by iteration 8, compared to the initial trajectory. In both cases, the resulting GP-MLMPC performance is on par with the full-model NMPC, which shows that the optimal controller can be learned by the approach. By collecting samples around the optimal trajectory, the GP-MLMPC remains sample-efficient across iterations and achieves quick convergence. Thus, the proposed GP-MLMPC scheme presents a promising data-efficient approach for the control of nonlinear batch processes without mechanistic knowledge.

### [98] [Operational Feature Fingerprints of Graph Datasets via a White-Box Signal-Subspace Probe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22676)
*Yuchen Xiong,Swee Keong Yeap,Zhen Hong Ban*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出WG-SRC，一种白盒信号子空间探测方法，用于图神经网络节点分类的预测与数据集诊断。它用固定的图信号字典替代学习型消息传递，通过Fisher坐标选择、类别PCA子空间和闭式多岭回归进行分类，在六个数据集上取得有竞争力的结果，并生成可解释的特征指纹来诊断不同图数据集的行为模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图神经网络虽然实现了强节点分类性能，但其学习到的消息传递机制将自我属性、邻域平滑、高通图差异、类别几何和分类器边界纠缠在一种不透明的表示中，导致无法理解节点为何被分类以及数据集需要何种图学习机制。

Method: WG-SRC用固定的命名图信号字典（原始特征、行归一化和对称归一化低通传播、高通图差异）替代学习型消息传递，结合Fisher坐标选择、类PCA子空间、闭形式多岭回归分类和基于验证的分数融合，实现预测和分析的显式化。

Result: 在六个节点分类数据集上，WG-SRC与复现的图基线模型相比具有竞争力，在统一数据划分下实现平均正向增益。生成的"特征指纹"图集能够区分低通主导的Amazon图、混合高通和类别几何复杂的Chameleon行为、以及原始/边界敏感的WebKB图。

Conclusion: WG-SRC作为白盒图学习工具，通过预测性能验证其诊断结果。其特征指纹是内在分类器输出而非事后解释，为后续分析和数据集特定修改提供指导。机制性干预实验验证了高通块是否为可移除噪声、原始特征是否应保留、以及岭型边界修正何时重要。

Abstract: Graph neural networks achieve strong node-classification accuracy, but their learned message passing entangles ego attributes, neighborhood smoothing, high-pass graph differences, class geometry, and classifier boundaries in an opaque representation. This obscures why a node is classified and what feature-level graph-learning mechanisms a dataset requires.
  We propose WG-SRC, a white-box signal-subspace probe for prediction and graph dataset diagnosis. WG-SRC replaces learned message passing with a fixed, named graph-signal dictionary of raw features, row-normalized and symmetric-normalized low-pass propagation, and high-pass graph differences. It combines Fisher coordinate selection, class-wise PCA subspaces, closed-form multi-alpha ridge classification, and validation-based score fusion, so prediction and analysis use explicit class subspaces, energy-controlled dimensions, and closed-form linear decisions.
  As a white-box graph-learning instrument, WG-SRC uses predictive performance to validate its diagnostics: across six node-classification datasets, the scaffold remains competitive with reproduced graph baselines and achieves positive average gain under aligned splits. Its atlas, produced by a predictor, decomposes behavior into raw-feature, low-pass, high-pass, class-geometric, and ridge-boundary components. These operational feature fingerprints distinguish low-pass-dominated Amazon graphs, mixed high-pass and class-geometrically complex Chameleon behavior, and raw- or boundary-sensitive WebKB graphs. As intrinsic classifier outputs rather than post-hoc explanations, these fingerprints provide post-evaluation guidance for later analysis and dataset-specific modification. Aligned mechanistic interventions support this guidance by indicating when high-pass blocks act as removable noise, when raw features should be preserved, and when ridge-type boundary correction matters.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present a method for discovering morphological features in low-resource Bantu languages by combining cross-lingual transfer learning with unsupervised clustering. Applied to Giriama (nyf), a language with only 91 labeled paradigms, our pipeline discovers noun class assignments for 2,455 words and identifies two previously undocumented morphological patterns: an a- prefix variant for Class 2 (vowel coalescence - the merger of two adjacent vowels - of wa-, 95.1% consistency) and a contracted k'- prefix (98.5% consistency). External validation on 444 known Giriama verb paradigms confirms 78.2% lemmatization accuracy, while a v3 corpus expansion to 19,624 words (9,014 unique lemmas) achieves 97.3% segmentation and 86.7% lemmatization rates across all major word classes. Our ensemble of transfer learning from Swahili and unsupervised clustering, combined via weighted voting, exploits complementary strengths: transfer excels at cognate detection (leveraging ~60% vocabulary overlap) while clustering discovers language-specific innovations invisible to transfer. We release all code and discovered lexicons to support morphological documentation for low-resource Bantu languages.

### [100] [Neural Recovery of Historical Lexical Structure in Bantu Languages from Modern Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22730)
*Hillary Mutisya,John Mugane*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文训练了一个基于班图语形态范式的Transformer模型（BantuMorph v7），发现其能从现代形态数据中自动恢复与历史重建一致的跨语言词汇结构，包括识别出与原始班图语高度匹配的同源词候选（名词90.9%准确率）以及符合Guthrie分类的系统发育分组。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究仅使用现代形态数据训练的神经模型是否能够恢复与历史语言学重建一致的跨语言词汇结构，从而验证神经网络能否捕捉到深层的历史语言关系。

Method: 使用BantuMorph v7（基于班图形态范式的Transformer）分析14种东部和南部班图语，提取名词和动词词条的编码器嵌入，识别跨5种以上语言的同源词候选，并分别与BLR3数据库和ASJP基础词汇进行比对验证，同时使用NLLB-600M翻译模型进行交叉验证。

Result: 名词同源候选的前11个中有10个（90.9%）对齐原始班图语重建形式；12个动词同源候选对齐原始班图语词根；两个独立模型均恢复出与Guthrie分类一致的语系分组（p<0.01）；13个名词类别的跨语言余弦相似度均>0.83。

Conclusion: 神经模型能够从现代形态数据中恢复与原始班图语一致的共享词汇结构，但受限于数据范围（仅东部和南部班图语），尚不能明确区分原始班图语保留特征与后期区域创新。

Abstract: We investigate whether neural models trained exclusively on modern morphological data can recover cross-lingual lexical structure consistent with historical reconstruction. Using BantuMorph v7, a transformer over Bantu morphological paradigms, we analyze 14 Eastern and Southern Bantu languages, extract encoder embeddings for their noun and verb lemmas, and identify 728 noun and 1,525 verb cognate candidates shared across 5+ languages. Evaluating these candidates against established historical resources-the Bantu Lexical Reconstructions database (BLR3; 4,786 reconstructed Proto-Bantu forms) and the ASJP basic vocabulary-we confirm 10 of the top 11 noun candidates (90.9%) align with previously reconstructed Proto-Bantu forms, including *-ntU 'person' (8 languages), *gombe 'cow' (9 languages), and *mUn (9 languages). Extending to verbs, 12 verb cognates align with reconstructed Proto-Bantu roots, including *-bon- 'see' and *-jIm- 'stand', each attested across wide geographic ranges. Cross-model validation using an independent translation model (NLLB-600M) confirms these patterns: both models recover cognate clusters and phylogenetic groupings consistent with established Guthrie-zone classifications (p < 0.01). Cross-lingual noun class analysis reveals that all 13 productive classes maintain >0.83 cosine similarity across languages (within-class > between-class, p < 10^-9). Our dataset is restricted to Eastern and Southern Bantu, so we interpret these results as recovering shared Bantu lexical structure consistent with Proto-Bantu rather than definitively distinguishing Proto-Bantu retentions from later regional innovations.

</details>


### [101] [Spend Less, Fit Better: Budget-Efficient Scaling Law Fitting via Active Experiment Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22753)
*Sijie Li,Shanda Li,Haowei Lin,Weiwei Sun,Ameet Talwalkar,Yiming Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将标度律拟合视为预算感知的序贯实验设计问题，通过不确定性感知方法高效分配实验预算，仅用约10%的总训练预算即可达到接近全实验集拟合的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标度律拟合的成本极高，传统方法将收集足够多的试点实验视为预处理步骤，但在现代大规模训练中这已成为主要的预算分配问题。现有方法缺乏对实验成本的感知，导致预算分配效率低下。

Method: 将标度律拟合形式化为预算感知的序贯实验设计问题，提出不确定性感知方法，在有限预算下序贯选择最有助于目标区域外推的实验运行。

Result: 在多种标度律任务基准上，该方法一致优于经典设计基线，仅用约10%总训练预算即可接近全实验集拟合的性能。

Conclusion: 标度律拟合中引入预算感知和序贯实验设计能大幅降低实验成本，为大规模训练预算分配提供了更高效的方案。

Abstract: Scaling laws are used to plan multi-million-dollar training runs, but fitting those laws can itself cost millions. In modern large-scale workflows, assembling a sufficiently informative set of pilot experiments is already a major budget-allocation problem rather than a routine preprocessing step. We formulate scaling-law fitting as budget-aware sequential experimental design: given a finite pool of runnable experiments with heterogeneous costs, choose which runs to execute so as to maximize extrapolation accuracy in a high-cost target region. We then propose an uncertainty-aware method for sequentially allocating experimental budget toward the runs most useful for target-region extrapolation. Across a diverse benchmark of scaling-law tasks, our method consistently outperforms classical design-based baselines, and often approaches the performance of fitting on the full experimental set while using only about 10% of the total training budget. Our code is available at https://github.com/PlanarG/active-sl.

</details>

### [102] [Aligning Dense Retrievers with LLM Utility via DistillationAligning Dense Retrievers with LLM Utility via Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22722)
*Rajinder Sandhu,Di Mu,Cheng Chang,Md Shahriar Tasjid,Himanshu Rai,Maksims Volkovs,Ga Wu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出Utility-Aligned Embeddings (UAE)框架，通过将检索建模为分布匹配问题，利用Utility-Modulated InfoNCE目标训练双编码器模拟基于困惑度降低的效用分布，在不引入测试时LLM推理的情况下将分级效用信号注入嵌入空间，在QASPER基准上显著提升检索性能，且速度比LLM重排序方法快180倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密集向量检索在RAG中广泛应用但精度有限，而基于LLM重排序的效用方法性能虽优但计算开销大且易受困惑度估计噪声影响。作者旨在融合两者优势，提出一种既高效又高性能的实用检索方法。

Method: 将检索形式化为分布匹配问题，训练双编码器（bi-encoder）以模仿基于困惑度降低导出的效用分布，使用Utility-Modulated InfoNCE目标函数，将分级效用信号直接注入嵌入空间，无需测试时调用LLM。

Result: 在QASPER基准上，UAE相比强语义基线BGE-Base，Retrieval Recall@1提升30.59%，MAP提升30.16%，Token F1提升17.3%。同时，UAE比高效的LLM重排序方法快180倍以上，同时保持竞争性性能。

Conclusion: 将检索与生成效用对齐能够在规模上提供可靠的上下文，证明了在不牺牲效率的前提下大幅提升检索精度的可行性。

Abstract: Dense vector retrieval is the practical backbone of Retrieval- Augmented Generation (RAG), but similarity search can suffer from precision limitations. Conversely, utility-based approaches leveraging LLM re-ranking often achieve superior performance but are computationally prohibitive and prone to noise inherent in perplexity estimation. We propose Utility-Aligned Embeddings (UAE), a framework designed to merge these advantages into a practical, high-performance retrieval method. We formulate retrieval as a distribution matching problem, training a bi-encoder to imitate a utility distribution derived from perplexity reduction using a Utility-Modulated InfoNCE objective. This approach injects graded utility signals directly into the embedding space without requiring test-time LLM inference. On the QASPER benchmark, UAE improves retrieval Recall@1 by 30.59%, MAP by 30.16% and Token F1 by 17.3% over the strong semantic baseline BGE-Base. Crucially, UAE is over 180x faster than the efficient LLM re-ranking methods preserving competitive performance, demonstrating that aligning retrieval with generative utility yields reliable contexts at scale.

</details>

### [103] [The Exact Replica Threshold for Nonlinear Moments of Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22627)
*Shuai Zeng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了在量子态复制品数量限制的联合测量模型中，估计 $\operatorname{tr}(ρ^t)$ 所需复制品数的精确阈值为 $\lceil t/2\rceil$：少于该阈值会导致随维度增长的样本复杂度，达到该阈值则可用多项式样本完成估计。该阈值规律还推广到可观测量加权矩 $\operatorname{tr}(Oρ^t)$ 族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究量子态多副本联合测量中，复制品数量（replica number）是否构成一个尖锐的信息论资源边界——即是否存在一个精确的阈值，少于该数量会导致样本复杂度随系统维度增长，而达到该数量则只需多项式样本。

Method: 通过理论证明：对于任意固定阶数 $t\ge 3$，在复制品数量限制的联合测量模型（sample/copy-access model with replica-limited joint measurements）中，证明 $\lceil t/2\rceil-1$ 个复制品必然需要随维度增长的样本复杂度，而 $\lceil t/2\rceil$ 个复制品（基于已有工作）足以用多项式样本估计 $\operatorname{tr}(ρ^t)$。并将该阈值规律推广到可观测量加权矩 $\operatorname{tr}(Oρ^t)$。

Result: 确定了固定阶纯矩的精确复制品阈值为 $\lceil t/2\rceil$；证明了该阈值规律同样适用于可观测量加权矩族（包括Pauli可观测量等）。

Conclusion: 相干复制品数量（coherent replica number）构成非线性量子态估计中一个真正的离散资源——额外一个相干复制品不仅是有用的，而且标志着多项式样本估计与维度增长样本复杂度之间的精确分界线。

Abstract: Joint measurements on multiple copies of a quantum state provide access to nonlinear observables such as $\operatorname{tr}(ρ^t)$, but whether replica number marks a sharp information-theoretic resource boundary has remained unclear. For every fixed order $t\ge 3$, existing protocols show that $\lceil t/2\rceil$ replicas already suffice for polynomial-sample estimation of $\operatorname{tr}(ρ^t)$, yet it has remained open whether one fewer replica must necessarily incur a sample-complexity barrier growing with the dimension. We prove that this is indeed the case in the sample/copy-access model with replica-limited joint measurements: any protocol restricted to $\lceil t/2\rceil-1$ replicas requires dimension-growing sample complexity, while $\lceil t/2\rceil$ replicas suffice by prior work. Thus the exact replica threshold for fixed-order pure moments is $\lceil t/2\rceil$. Equivalently, for fixed-order pure moments, one additional coherent replica is not merely useful but marks the exact threshold between polynomial-sample estimation and a dimension-growing regime in the replica-limited model. We further show that the same threshold law extends to a broad family of observable-weighted moments $\operatorname{tr}(Oρ^t)$, including Pauli observables and other observables with bounded operator norm and macroscopic trace norm. Coherent replica number therefore acts as a genuinely discrete resource for nonlinear quantum-state estimation.

</details>

### [104] [Wiggle and Go! System Identification for Zero-Shot Dynamic Rope Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22102)
*Arthur Jakobsson,Abhinav Mahajan,Karthik Pullalarevu,Krishna Suresh,Yunchao Yao,Yuemin Mao,Bardienus Duisterhof,Shahram Najam Syed,Jeffrey Ichnowski*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出Wiggle and Go!框架，利用学习的仿真先验实现零样本动态绳索操控，通过系统辨识模块预测物理参数并指导优化方法，在真实环境中达到3.55cm的平均3D目标打击精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态绳索操控任务容错率低，现有方法依赖大规模真实数据集或迭代尝试，无法实现零样本高效执行。

Method: 两阶段框架：1) 系统辨识模块观测绳索运动预测物理参数；2) 基于这些参数的目标条件优化方法预测机器人动作，零样本在真实世界执行。

Result: 真实环境3D目标打击平均精度3.55cm（对比无系统参数时的15.34cm）；预测与真实绳索的傅里叶频率Pearson相关系数达0.95。

Conclusion: 任务无关的系统辨识模块可无缝切换多种动态绳索操控任务，实现零样本高效执行，显著优于无参数感知的方法。

Abstract: Many robotic tasks are unforgiving; a single mistake in a dynamic throw can lead to unacceptable delays or unrecoverable failure. To mitigate this, we present a novel approach that leverages learned simulation priors to inform goal-conditioned dynamic manipulation of ropes for efficient and accurate task execution. Related methods for dynamic rope manipulation either require large real-world datasets to estimate rope behavior or the use of iterative improvements on attempts at the task for goal completion. We introduce Wiggle and Go!, a system-identification, two-stage framework that enables zero-shot task rope manipulation. The framework consists of a system identification module that observes rope movement to predict descriptive physical parameters, which then informs an optimization method for goal-conditioned action prediction for the robot to execute zero-shot in the real. Our method achieves strong performance across multiple dynamic manipulation tasks enabled by the same task-agnostic system identification module which offers seamless switching between different manipulation tasks, allowing a single model to support a diverse array of manipulation policies. We achieve a 3.55 cm average accuracy on 3D target striking in real using rope system parameters in comparison to 15.34 cm accuracy when our task model is not system-parameter-informed. We achieve a Pearson correlation coefficient of 0.95 between Fourier frequencies of the predicted and real ropes on an unseen trajectory. Project website please see https://wiggleandgo.github.io/

</details>


### [105] [Learning-augmented robotic automation for real-world manufacturing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22235)
*Yunho Kim,Quan Nguyen,Taewhan Kim,Youngjin Heo,Joonho Lee*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了学习增强型机器人自动化（LARA）系统，将学习型任务控制器与神经3D安全监控器集成到传统工业流程中，在电动马达生产线上成功实现了变形的电缆插入和焊接自动化。仅需不到20分钟的真实数据训练，系统连续运行5小时10分钟，生产108个马达，通过率达99.4%，且无需物理围栏，证明基于学习的方法可实际应用于工业自动化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业机器人虽广泛使用，但多数操控仍依赖固定脚本，对环境变化脆弱。基于学习的控制方法更具适应性，但尚未在真实生产线中验证其能否长时间可靠运行、保持一致质量并在人员周围安全操作。本文旨在弥合这一差距。

Method: 提出LARA混合系统，结合学习型任务控制器和神经3D安全监控器，集成到传统工业工作流程中。在电动马达生产线上部署，用于自动化变形电缆插入和焊接任务，仅需不到20分钟的真实世界数据即可训练。

Result: 系统连续运行5小时10分钟，生产108个马达，无需物理围栏，产品级质量控制测试通过率99.4%，保持接近人类的生产节拍时间，同时减少了焊接质量和循环时间的变异性。

Conclusion: 该结果证明了基于学习的方法可以实际扩展到工业自动化中，为工业机器人的智能化改造提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Industrial robots are widely used in manufacturing, yet most manipulation still depends on fixed waypoint scripts that are brittle to environmental changes. Learning-based control offers a more adaptive alternative, but it remains unclear whether such methods, still mostly confined to laboratory demonstrations, can sustain hours of reliable operation, deliver consistent quality, and behave safely around people on a live production line. Here we present Learning-Augmented Robotic Automation, a hybrid system that integrates learned task controllers and a neural 3D safety monitor into conventional industrial workflows. We deployed the system on an electric-motor production line to automate deformable cable insertion and soldering under real manufacturing constraints, a step previously performed manually by human workers. With less than 20 min of real-world data per task, the system operated continuously for 5 h 10 min, producing 108 motors without physical fencing and achieving a 99.4% pass rate on product-level quality-control tests. It maintained near-human takt time while reducing variability in solder-joint quality and cycle time. These results establish a practical pathway for extending industrial automation with learning-based methods.

### [106] [Conditional Diffusion Posterior Alignment for Sparse-View CT Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21960)
*Luis Barba,Johannes Kirschner,Benjamin Bejar*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出条件扩散后验对齐（CDPA）方法，通过条件化2D扩散模型于初始3D重建并结合数据一致性对齐，实现了大规模3D稀疏视角CT重建，在合成和真实CBCT数据上达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度扩散模型在稀疏视角CT重建中难以扩展到大型3D体积，主要原因有三：3D模型内存和计算需求高、缺乏大规模3D训练数据、独立使用2D模型导致切片间不一致。本文旨在克服这些限制。

Method: 提出条件扩散后验对齐（CDPA），使用2D U-Net扩散模型，以初始3D重建结果为条件以改善切片间一致性，再结合数据一致性对齐（与测量投影匹配）进行后处理。

Result: 在合成和真实锥束CT（CBCT）数据上达到SOTA性能；消融实验证实各模块的协同效应；该方法还可增强快速去噪U-Net，以极低计算成本获得接近扩散模型的质量。

Conclusion: CDPA成功将扩散模型扩展到大规模3D稀疏视角CT重建，通过条件化和数据一致性对齐克服了内存、数据和切片不一致三大限制，并展示了其通用性可提升快速模型的性能。

Abstract: Computed Tomography (CT) is a widely used imaging modality in medical and industrial applications. To limit radiation exposure and measurement time, there is a growing interest in sparse-view CT, where the number of projection views is significantly reduced. Deep neural networks have shown great promise in improving reconstruction quality in sparse-view CT, especially generative diffusion models. However, these methods struggle to scale to large 3D volumes due to several reasons: (i) the high memory and computational requirements of 3D models, (ii) the lack of large 3D training datasets, and (iii) the inconsistencies across slices when using 2D models independently on each slice. We overcome these limitations and scale diffusion-based sparse-view CT reconstruction to large 3D volumes by combining conditional diffusion with explicit data consistency. We propose Conditional Diffusion Posterior Alignment (CDPA) to enable scalable 3D sparse-view CT reconstruction. A 2D U-Net diffusion model is conditioned on an initial 3D reconstruction to improve inter-slice consistency, combined with data-consistency alignment to match measured projections. Experiments on synthetic and real Cone Beam CT (CBCT) data show state-of-the-art performance, with ablations that confirm the synergistic effects of the proposed pipeline. Finally, we show that the same principles also strengthen fast denoising U-Nets, yielding near-diffusion quality at a fraction of the computational cost.

</details>


### [107] [Multimodal Diffusion to Mutually Enhance Polarized Light and Low Resolution EBSD Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22212)
*Harry Dong,Timofey Efimov,Megna Shah,Jeff Simmons,Sean Donegan,Marc De Graef,Yuejie Chi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3D-EBSD数据采集过程耗时，需要寻找偏振光等其他模态来加速采集，同时利用共享信息补充数据。

Method: 使用无条件多模态扩散模型，在合成数据上训练一次，即可泛化到真实数据，支持低分辨率、噪声、损坏和未配准的数据。

Result: 仅需25%的EBSD数据（1/4分辨率）加上受损的PL数据，即可达到接近全分辨率的表现。

Conclusion: 该扩散模型在晶界预测、超分辨率和去噪等任务上表现优异，具有强泛化能力和推理时缩放增益。

Abstract: In spite of the utility of 3-D electron back-scattered diffraction (EBSD) microscopy, the data collection process can be time-consuming with serial-sectioning. Hence, it is natural to look at other modalities, such as polarized light (PL) data, to accelerate EBSD data collection, supplemented with shared information. Complementarily, features in chaotic PL data could even be enriched with a handful of EBSD measurements. To inherently learn the complex dynamics between EBSD and PL to solve these inverse problems, we use an unconditional multimodal diffusion model, motivated by progress in diffusion models for inverse problems. Although trained solely on synthetic data once, our model has strong generalizable capabilities on real data which can be low-resolution, noisy, corrupted, and misregistered. With inference-time scaling, we show gains in performance on a variety of objectives including grain boundary prediction, super-resolution, and denoising. With our model, we demonstrate that there is little difference from full resolution performance with only 25% (1/4 the resolution) of EBSD data and corrupted PL data.

</details>


### [108] [Are Natural-Domain Foundation Models Effective for Accelerated Cardiac MRI Reconstruction?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22557)
*Anam Hashmi,Mayug Maniparambil,Julia Dietlmeier,Kathleen M. Curran,Noel E. O'Connor*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文探索了大规模预训练基础模型（如CLIP、DINOv2、BiomedCLIP）作为图像先验用于加速心脏MRI重建的效果，提出了一种展开式重建框架。实验表明，虽然任务专用模型（如E2E-VarNet）在标准分布内表现更优，但基础模型在跨域场景下展现出更强的鲁棒性和泛化能力，尤其是高加速因子和低频采样受限时。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模预训练基础模型在计算机视觉下游任务中表现优异，但它们在基于物理的反问题（如加速心脏MRI重建）中的应用潜力尚未被充分探索。本文旨在研究自然域基础模型能否作为有效的图像先验用于加速心脏MRI重建，并与领域专用模型（如BiomedCLIP）进行对比。

Method: 提出一种展开式（unrolled）重建框架，在每个级联模块中引入预训练的、冻结的视觉编码器（CLIP、DINOv2、BiomedCLIP）来引导重建过程。通过冻结编码器参数，保留其预训练的知识作为图像先验。

Result: ① 任务专用模型（E2E-VarNet）在标准分布内表现最优；② 基础模型方法在标准设置下具有竞争力；③ 在挑战性跨域场景（心脏MRI训练→膝盖/脑部MRI测试）中，基础模型展现出更强的鲁棒性，尤其在高加速因子和低频采样受限时；④ 自然图像预训练模型（CLIP）学习到高度可迁移的结构表征；⑤ 领域专用预训练（BiomedCLIP）在更病态条件下提供适度额外增益。

Conclusion: 预训练基础模型为加速MRI重建提供了有前景的可迁移先验，能够提升模型的鲁棒性和泛化能力，特别是在跨域和极端采样条件下。

Abstract: The emergence of large-scale pretrained foundation models has transformed computer vision, enabling strong performance across diverse downstream tasks. However, their potential for physics-based inverse problems, such as accelerated cardiac MRI reconstruction, remains largely underexplored. In this work, we investigate whether natural-domain foundation models can serve as effective image priors for accelerated cardiac MRI reconstruction, and compare the performance obtained against domain-specific counterparts such as BiomedCLIP. We propose an unrolled reconstruction framework that incorporates pretrained, frozen visual encoders, such as CLIP, DINOv2, and BiomedCLIP, within each cascade to guide the reconstruction process. Through extensive experiments, we show that while task-specific state-of-the-art reconstruction models such as E2E-VarNet achieve superior performance in standard in-distribution settings, foundation-model-based approaches remain competitive. More importantly, in challenging cross-domain scenarios, where models are trained on cardiac MRI and evaluated on anatomically distinct knee and brain datasets--foundation models exhibit improved robustness, particularly under high acceleration factors and limited low-frequency sampling. We further observe that natural-image-pretrained models, such as CLIP, learn highly transferable structural representations, while domain-specific pretraining (BiomedCLIP) provides modest additional gains in more ill-posed regimes. Overall, our results suggest that pretrained foundation models offer a promising source of transferable priors, enabling improved robustness and generalization in accelerated MRI reconstruction.

</details>


### [109] [Useful nonrobust features are ubiquitous in biomedical images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22579)
*Coenraad Mouton,Randle Rabe,Niklas C. Koser,Nicolai Krekiehn,Christopher Hansen,Jan-Bernd Hövener,Claus-C. Glüer*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了医学影像深度网络是否学习到“非鲁棒特征”——这些特征虽不可解释且易受微小扰动影响，但具有预测价值。实验表明，仅用非鲁棒特征训练的模型在MedMNIST任务中仍表现良好，而对抗训练模型虽牺牲了分布内精度，但在分布偏移下表现更优，揭示了医学影像分类中鲁棒性与准确率的实际权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究医学影像深度网络是否学习到非鲁棒特征（人类不可解释但具预测性的输入模式），以及这些特征如何影响测试性能，特别是在分布偏移下的表现。

Method: 在五个MedMNIST分类任务上，对比仅用非鲁棒特征训练的模型与对抗训练（依赖鲁棒特征）的模型，分析它们在分布内精度和受控分布偏移（MedMNIST-C）下的表现差异。

Result: 仅用非鲁棒特征训练的模型在分布内达到高于偶然水平的准确率；对抗训练模型牺牲了分布内精度，但在分布偏移下表现显著更好。

Conclusion: 非鲁棒特征提升了标准准确率但降低了分布外性能，揭示了医学影像分类中鲁棒性与准确率之间的实际权衡，应根据部署场景需求进行针对性设计。

Abstract: We study whether deep networks for medical imaging learn useful nonrobust features - predictive input patterns that are not human interpretable and highly susceptible to small adversarial perturbations - and how these features impact test performance. We show that models trained only on nonrobust features achieve well above chance accuracy across five MedMNIST classification tasks, confirming their predictive value in-distribution. Conversely, adversarially trained models that primarily rely on robust features sacrifice in-distribution accuracy but yield markedly better performance under controlled distribution shifts (MedMNIST-C). Overall, nonrobust features boost standard accuracy yet degrade out-of-distribution performance, revealing a practical robustness-accuracy trade-off in medical imaging classification tasks that should be tailored to the requirements of the deployment setting.

</details>

### [110] [AutoINV: Automated Invariant Generation Framework for Formal Verification on High-Level Synthesis Designs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22285)
*Xiaofeng Zhou,Linfeng Du,Guangyu Hu,Sharad Sinha,Hongce Zhang,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出利用HLS流程中的高层设计特征构建helper assertions，通过迭代重用证明信息选择最有效的helper集合，加速HLS生成RTL设计的模型检验，平均加速2.23倍，最高6.05倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HLS工具生成的RTL设计可能存在功能错误或安全漏洞，而模型检验作为最可靠的验证方法之一，常因生成的RTL规模过大而难以在合理时间内完成验证。

Method: 利用HLS流程中的高层设计特征构建一组helper assertions，并开发了一种迭代重用证明信息的机制，选择对模型检验最有帮助的断言子集来加速验证过程。

Result: 在HLS设计基准测试上，相比原始模型检验，该方法实现了最高6.05倍、平均2.23倍的加速。

Conclusion: 利用HLS高层设计特征构建的helper assertions能够有效指导模型检验器，显著加速HLS生成RTL的验证过程。

Abstract: High-level synthesis (HLS) transforms an algorithmic description of hardware from a higher abstraction (e.g., C/C++) into a register-transfer level (RTL) design, offering reduced development time and greater flexibility in design space exploration. However, such machine-generated RTL designs may contain major functional bugs or security vulnerabilities due to limitations or errors in the HLS tools. One of the most reliable methods to identify these vulnerabilities is formal verification, particularly model checking. Nevertheless, the large size of the generated RTL often causes model checking to struggle to conclude within reasonable time or resource limits.
  In this study, we propose utilizing the high-level design features from the HLS flow to construct a set of helper assertions aimed at guiding the model checker and accelerating the verification process. To identify the most effective set of helpers to assist the model checker, we develop a proving mechanism that iteratively reuses proving information to select the potentially most useful set of helpers.
  We evaluate the proposed framework on a set of HLS design benchmarks. Experimental results demonstrate that, when compared to vanilla model checking, our approach achieves a speedup of up to 6.05x, and 2.23x on average.

</details>


### [111] [HGQ-LUT: Fast LUT-Aware Training and Efficient Architectures for DNN Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22293)
*Chang Sun,Zhiqiang Que,Bakhtiar Zadeh,Qibin Liu,Kevin H. Alvarez,Wayne Luk,Maria Spiropulu*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: HGQ-LUT是一种新型LUT感知训练方法，通过引入LUT-Dense和LUT-Conv层，利用常规张量运算加速训练超100倍，并实现自动精度-资源权衡，已在CERN大型强子对撞机等实际场景中验证可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LUT感知训练方法训练速度慢（慢数个数量级）、需要繁琐的手动调参以获得硬件效率、缺乏端到端工作流，难以在实际中部署使用。

Method: 提出LUT-Dense和LUT-Conv层，训练时用常规高效的张量运算实现，而后编译为逻辑LUT；结合细粒度异构量化（包括零比特剪枝）和LUT感知的资源代理函数，实现精度-资源权衡的自动探索；集成到开源工具链，支持混合架构的统一设计、编译和位精确验证。

Result: 在GPU上训练速度提升超过100倍；在硬件效率上达到最先进水平；实现了自动化的精度-资源权衡探索，无需手动调整位宽；成功部署于CERN大型强子对撞机实验等真实场景。

Conclusion: HGQ-LUT使得基于LUT的深度神经网络在现实部署中变得实用，解决了之前方法在训练速度、自动化程度和工具链完整性方面的关键瓶颈，为FPGA上的低延迟推理提供了可行的端到端解决方案。

Abstract: Lookup-table (LUT) based neural networks can deliver ultra-low latency and excellent hardware efficiency on FPGAs by mapping arithmetic operations directly onto the logic primitives. However, state-of-the-art LUT-aware training (LAT) approaches remain difficult to use in practice: they are often orders of magnitude slower to train than conventional networks, require non-trivial manual tuning for hardware efficiency, and lack an end-to-end workflow. This work presents HGQ-LUT, integrated in https://github.com/calad0i/HGQ2, a new LAT approach that achieves state-of-the-art hardware efficiency while accelerating training by over 100 times on modern GPUs. HGQ-LUT introduces LUT-Dense and LUT-Conv layers that are implemented with regular, accelerator-efficient tensor operations during training, which are then compiled into logic LUTs for hardware. By combining these layers with fine-grained, element-wise heterogeneous quantization (including zero-bit pruning) and a LUT-aware resource surrogate, HGQ-LUT enables the automatic exploration of accuracy-resource trade-offs without manual bit-width tuning. We further integrate HGQ-LUT into open-source toolchains, enabling unified design, compilation, and bit-exact verification of hybrid architectures that mix LUT-based with conventional arithmetic blocks. These features make LAT-based DNNs practical for real-world deployment, such as at the CERN Large Hadron Collider's experiments.

</details>

### [112] [Near-Optimal Regret for the Safe Learning-based Control of the Constrained Linear Quadratic Regulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22158)
*Spencer Hutchinson,Nanfei Jiang,Mahnoosh Alizadeh*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了带约束的随机线性二次型调节器（LQR）的自适应控制问题，提出了一种基于SDP选择乐观策略并"回缩"至安全策略的算法，实现了$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$的遗憾界和机会约束满足，其中关键是通过协方差分析而非传统代价分析来建立理论保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前在多维带约束LQR问题中仅能达到$\tilde{O}(T^{2/3})$的遗憾界，且只能处理鲁棒约束。本文旨在探索是否能将遗憾界提升至$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$，同时放宽约束类型以处理无界噪声。

Method: 提出一种基于SDP（半定规划）的算法：首先选择乐观策略，然后将该策略"回缩"至可验证安全的策略。核心创新在于利用协方差分析（而非传统的代价分析）来建立理论保证。

Result: 实现了$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$的遗憾界，并满足机会约束（概率意义上的约束）。与先前工作的$\tilde{O}(T^{2/3})$遗憾界和鲁棒约束相比，取得了显著的改进。

Conclusion: 通过协方差分析这一新颖视角，证明了在带约束的随机LQR中可以实现$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$的遗憾界，并处理更具一般性的机会约束（允许无界噪声），为自适应LQR提供了新的理论分析框架。

Abstract: We study the problem of adaptive control of the stochastic linear quadratic regulator (LQR) with constraints that must be satisfied at every time step. Prior work on the multidimensional problem has shown $\tilde{O}(T^{2/3})$ regret and satisfaction of robust constraints, leaving open the question of whether $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret can be attained in the constrained LQR setting. We contribute to this problem by showing $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret and satisfaction of chance constraints. This type of constraints allow us to handle unbounded noise and also enable analytical techniques not directly applicable to robust constraints. Our proposed algorithm for this problem uses an SDP to select an optimistic policy, and then "scales back" this policy until it is verifiably-safe. Our theoretical analysis establishes regret and constraint guarantees via a key lemma that bounds the system covariance in terms of the chosen policy. This covariance-based analysis is in contrast with the cost-to-go based analysis that is typically used in adaptive LQR.

</details>


### [113] [Relaxation-Informed Training of Neural Network Surrogate Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22746)
*Calvin Tsay*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出针对ReLU神经网络训练的专用正则化方法，通过惩罚MILP重构中的big-M常数、不稳定神经元数量以及LP松弛间隙，将下游MILP求解效率提升多达四个数量级，同时保持代理模型精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准训练目标（预测损失+经典权重正则化）无法直接控制训练后网络嵌入MILP的可解性（二进制变量数量、LP松弛紧度），导致优化求解困难。需要设计能直接优化下游MILP可解性的训练正则化器。

Method: 1) 基于边界的正则化器：惩罚big-M常数和不稳定神经元数量；2) LP松弛间隙正则化器：通过LP对偶变量计算梯度，显式惩罚训练点处连续松弛的每样本间隙；3) 组合正则化器近似LP间隙对网络参数的全导数，捕获直接与间接敏感性。

Result: 在非凸基准函数和两阶段随机规划问题上，相比未正则化的基线，MILP求解时间最多降低四个数量级，且代理模型精度具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 通过训练阶段引入面向MILP可解性的正则化，可以在不牺牲模型精度的情况下大幅提升下游优化问题的求解效率，为神经网络嵌入优化提供实用训练策略。

Abstract: ReLU neural networks trained as surrogate models can be embedded exactly in mixed-integer linear programs (MILPs), enabling global optimization over the learned function. The tractability of the resulting MILP depends on structural properties of the network, i.e., the number of binary variables in associated formulations and the tightness of the continuous LP relaxation. These properties are determined during training, yet standard training objectives (prediction loss with classical weight regularization) offer no mechanism to directly control them. This work studies training regularizers that directly target downstream MILP tractability. Specifically, we propose simple bound-based regularizers that penalize the big-M constants of MILP formulations and/or the number of unstable neurons. Moreover, we introduce an LP relaxation gap regularizer that explicitly penalizes the per-sample gap of the continuous relaxation at training points. We derive its associated gradient and provide an implementation from LP dual variables without custom automatic differentiation tools. We show that combining the above regularizers can approximate the full total derivative of the LP gap with respect to the network parameters, capturing both direct and indirect sensitivities. Experiments on non-convex benchmark functions and a two-stage stochastic programming problem with quantile neural network surrogates demonstrate that the proposed regularizers can reduce MILP solve times by up to four orders of magnitude relative to an unregularized baseline, while maintaining competitive surrogate model accuracy.

</details>

### [114] [MambaCSP: Hybrid-Attention State Space Models for Hardware-Efficient Channel State Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21957)
*Aladin Djuhera,Haris Gacanin,Holger Boche*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出MambaCSP，一种混合注意力状态空间模型，用于CSI预测，在保持高精度的同时大幅提升计算效率和推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer/LLM的CSI预测方法虽能捕捉长程时序依赖，但存在序列长度的二次方缩放问题，导致计算成本高、内存消耗大、推理延迟长，难以应用于实时和资源受限的无线场景。

Method: 提出MambaCSP架构：采用线性时间的Mamba（选择性状态空间模型）替代LLM预测主干，并引入轻量级patch-mixer注意力层，周期性注入跨token注意力以弥补纯SSM仅能捕捉局部依赖的不足。

Result: 在MISO-OFDM仿真中，MambaCSP相比LLM方法：预测精度提升9-12%，吞吐量提升3.0倍，VRAM使用降低2.6倍，推理速度提升2.9倍。

Conclusion: 混合状态空间架构为未来无线网络中的可扩展、硬件高效的AI原生CSI预测提供了有前景的方向。

Abstract: Recent works have demonstrated that attention-based transformer and large language model (LLM) architectures can achieve strong channel state prediction (CSP) performance by capturing long-range temporal dependencies across channel state information (CSI) sequences. However, these models suffer from quadratic scaling in sequence length, leading to substantial computational cost, memory consumption, and inference latency, which limits their applicability in real-time and resource-constrained wireless deployments. In this paper, we investigate whether selective state space models (SSMs) can serve as a hardware-efficient alternative for CSI prediction. We propose MambaCSP, a hybrid-attention SSM architecture that replaces LLM-based prediction backbones with a linear-time Mamba model. To overcome the local-only dependencies of pure SSMs, we introduce lightweight patch-mixer attention layers that periodically inject cross-token attentions, helping with long-context CSI prediction. Extensive MISO-OFDM simulations show that MambaCSP improves prediction accuracy over LLM-based approaches by 9-12%, while delivering up to 3.0x higher throughput, 2.6x lower VRAM usage, and 2.9x faster inference. Our results demonstrate that hybrid state space architectures provide a promising direction for scalable and hardware-efficient AI-native CSI prediction in future wireless networks.

</details>


### [115] [Null-Space Flow Matching for MIMO Channel Estimation in Latency-Constrained Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22005)
*Junjie Zhao,Guangming Liang,Dongzhu Liu,Xiaonan Liu*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种零空间流匹配框架，用于在低延迟约束下实现高精度的MIMO信道估计。该方法将信道估计分解为范围空间重建和零空间生成两部分，并引入幂律时间调度和噪声感知自适应校正策略，在约3ms延迟下取得了优于现有方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于深度生成模型（如分数模型、扩散模型）的CSI重建方法虽然精度高，但推理延迟大，难以满足低延迟通信系统的需求。因此，本文旨在在严格延迟约束下实现准确的信道估计。

Method: 提出零空间流匹配框架，将MIMO信道估计分解为：1）从含噪导频观测中直接恢复信道范围空间分量；2）利用流匹配生成先验迭代细化模糊的零空间分量。同时引入幂律时间调度优化有限细化步数的分配，以及噪声感知自适应校正策略抑制轨迹中的信道噪声。

Result: 在约3ms的严格延迟预算下，所提方法取得了有竞争力的归一化均方误差性能，在估计精度和推理速度上均优于基于模型和基于生成模型的基线方法。

Conclusion: 提出的零空间流匹配框架能够在低延迟约束下实现准确的信道估计，为MIMO通信系统中精确且低延迟的CSI获取提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Accurate yet low-latency channel state information (CSI) acquisition is essential for multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) communication systems. While advanced deep generative models, such as score-based and diffusion models, enable high-fidelity CSI reconstruction from limited pilot observations, they often suffer from high inference latency. To achieve accurate CSI estimation under stringent latency constraints, this paper proposes a null-space flow matching (FM) framework that decomposes pilot-limited MIMO channel estimation into a range-space reconstruction problem and a null-space generation problem. Specifically, the range-space component of the channel is directly recovered from noisy pilot observations, while only the ambiguous null-space component is iteratively refined using an FM-based generative prior. To further improve the robustness of the proposed framework, we introduce a power-law time schedule to better allocate the limited number of refinement steps, along with a noise-aware adaptive correction strategy to suppress channel noise on the refinement trajectory. Experimental results demonstrate that our method achieves a competitive normalized mean square error (NMSE) even under a strict latency budget of around 3 ms, while delivering superior estimation accuracy and faster inference than both model-based and generative baselines.

### [116] [Foundation models for discovering robust biomarkers of neurological disorders from dynamic functional connectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22018)
*Deepank Girish,Yi Hao Chan,Sukrit Gupta,Jing Xia,Jagath C. Rajapakse*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出RE-CONFIRM框架用于评估深度学习模型（包括脑基础模型）识别的生物标志物鲁棒性，并在此基础上提出Hub-LoRA微调方法，使基础模型不仅能超越定制化深度学习模型，还能产生经元分析验证的神经生物学可信生物标志物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脑基础模型在动态功能连接建模和疾病预测中表现优异，但其所识别的潜在生物标志物的鲁棒性尚未得到充分评估。常用的性能指标（如准确率）不足以评价模型发现的生物标志物是否可靠。

Method: 提出RE-CONFIRM评估框架，用于衡量深度学习模型（包括基础模型）所识别生物标志物的鲁棒性；并进一步提出Hub-LoRA微调方法，使基础模型能有效捕捉区域枢纽（regional hubs），生成神经生物学可信的生物标志物。

Result: 在五个大规模数据集（ASD、ADHD、AD）上的实验表明：常用性能指标不足以评估生物标志物鲁棒性；简单微调基础模型导致其无法有效捕捉区域枢纽；Hub-LoRA使基础模型既超越定制化模型，又产生经元分析验证的可信生物标志物。

Conclusion: RE-CONFIRM是一个通用且易于应用的评估框架，Hub-LoRA能有效提升基础模型在脑疾病应用中生物标志物的神经生物学保真度。

Abstract: Several brain foundation models (FM) have recently been proposed to predict brain disorders by modelling dynamic functional connectivity (FC). While they demonstrate remarkable model performance and zero- or few-shot generalization, the salient features identified as potential biomarkers are yet to be thoroughly evaluated. We propose RE-CONFIRM, a framework for evaluating the robustness of potential biomarker candidates elucidated by deep learning (DL) models including FMs. From experiments on five large datasets of Autism Spectrum Disorder (ASD), Attention-deficit Hyperactivity Disorder (ADHD), and Alzheimer's Disease (AD), we found that although commonly used performance metrics provide an intuitive assessment of model predictions, they are insufficient for evaluating the robustness of biomarkers identified by these models. RE-CONFIRM metrics revealed that simply finetuning FMs leads to models that fail to capture regional hubs effectively, even in disorders where hubs are known to be implicated, such as ASD and ADHD. In view of this, we propose Hub-LoRA (Low-Rank Adaptation) as a fine-tuning technique that enables FMs to not only outperform customised DL models but also produce neurobiologically faithful biomarkers supported by meta-analyses. RE-CONFIRM is generalizable and can be easily applied to ascertain the robustness of DL models trained on functional MRI datasets. Code is available at: https://github.com/SCSE-Biomedical-Computing-Group/RE-CONFIRM.

### [117] [Quantifying Interface Procedure Coupling Risks in Digital Nuclear Control Rooms: An Event Based Human Reliability Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21932)
*Xingyu Xiao,Mingwei Xiao,Hongbo Li,Jingang Liang,Jiejuan Tong,Haitao Wang*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本研究基于2021-2025年核电厂真实运行事件，提出三维标注框架和四因子界面机制模型，发现42.6%的事件存在界面缺陷，界面问题使程序偏差概率倍增，其中语义不匹配和布局诱导是耦合失效的主因，语义混淆占界面诱发错误的27.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字化已根本改变核主控室人机交互方式，但界面如何量化放大程序风险尚不明确，缺乏基于真实运行数据的系统性评估。

Method: 构建可复用的三维标注框架和四因子界面机制模型（布局、语义、不匹配、标注缺陷），结合机器学习解释和模拟器验证。

Result: 42.6%事件涉及界面缺陷，界面问题使程序偏差概率翻倍；语义混淆占界面诱发错误的27.3%，复合界面-程序耦合是失效主因。

Abstract: Digitalization has fundamentally transformed human system interaction in nuclear main control rooms, yet the quantitative mechanisms by which interfaces amplify procedural risks remain insufficiently understood. This study presents a systematic assessment of interface procedure coupling based on real operational events collected from 2021 to 2025 in a modern nuclear power plant. A reusable three dimensional labeling framework and a four factor interface mechanism model are developed to characterize layout, semantic, mismatch, and labeling deficiencies. Results show that interface issues function as a significant risk amplifier. A total of 42.6 percent of events involved interface deficiencies, and their presence more than doubled the likelihood of procedural deviation. Machine learning interpretation further reveals that composite interface procedure coupling, particularly driven by semantic mismatches and layout induced traps, is the dominant contributor to coupled failures. Simulator based validation confirms that semantic confusion accounts for 27.3 percent of interface induced errors, with overall error patterns consistent with historical data. The study provides a data driven HRA workflow for early vulnerability identification in digital control rooms and proposes a systematic framework for interface procedure semantic alignment to support risk informed design and verification.

### [118] [A Systematic AI Adoption Framework for Higher Education: From Student GenAI Usage to Institutional Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22030)
*Michael Neumann,Lasse Bischof,Maria Rauschenberger,Eva-Maria Schön*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI技术快速发展，学生学习中广泛使用，但大多数高校缺乏系统性机制来调整规章制度和课程以适应这一变化，导致监管模糊和学术诚信风险。

Method: 以德国汉诺威应用科学与艺术大学为案例，采用文档分析与在线问卷调查（N=151，面向商业信息系统和电子政务专业学生）相结合的方法。定量数据进行统计分析，开放式回答进行主题综合。

Result: ChatGPT是主导工具，学生主要用GenAI进行研究辅助、编程支持和文本处理。但政策不确定性显著，许多学生不了解或不确定学校的GenAI规定。文档分析揭示了规则漏洞、术语模糊以及正式规则与教学实践之间的不一致。

Despite increasing student adoption, many institutions lack operational mechanisms to systematically align regulations and curricula with evolving generative artificial intelligence practices, creating regulatory ambiguity and academic integrity risks. This study investigates how students utilize generative artificial intelligence tools in computer science-oriented disciplines and develops a structured, lightweight framework supporting institutional adaptation to pervasive GenAI usage. We conducted a case study at the University of Applied Sciences and Arts Hannover (Germany), combining document analysis with an online survey (N = 151) targeting Business Information Systems and E-Government students. Quantitative responses were analyzed statistically, while open-ended responses underwent thematic synthesis. Generative artificial intelligence adoption was widespread, with ChatGPT as the dominant tool. Students primarily used generative artificial intelligence for research assistance, programming support, and text processing. However, substantial policy uncertainty was observed: many students were unaware of or unsure about institutional generative artificial intelligence regulations. Document analysis revealed regulatory gaps, ambiguous terminology, and inconsistencies between formal rules and teaching practices. To address these shortcomings, we propose the AI Adoption Framework for Higher Education, an iterative and operational model integrating document analysis, empirical observation, synthesis of findings, and targeted updates of regulations and curricula. The framework addresses governance, assessment validity, and academic integrity under generative artificial intelligence conditions and provides practical guidance for institutional adaptation.

### [119] [Algorithmic Feature Highlighting for Human-AI Decision-Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22236)
*Yifan Guo,Jann Spiess*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究在人类决策者信息处理能力有限的情况下，如何通过算法高亮（highlighting）一小部分案例特定特征来辅助人类决策，并分析了不同认知水平的人类主体（复杂型vs.朴素型）对高亮策略的反应，揭示了优化复杂型主体的高亮策略在计算上不可行，而优化朴素型主体则可行，且为复杂型设计的最优策略在朴素型面前可能表现极差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类决策者面对复杂案例时，信息处理带宽有限，难以整合所有相关信息。传统算法往往直接给出预测或建议，但作者认为"高亮"关键特征比直接预测更能实现人机互补，因此需要系统研究高亮策略的优化问题。

Method: 将高亮建模为一种受约束的信息策略，选择少量特征向人类展示。区分两类人类主体：复杂型（能正确条件于选择规则）和朴素型（仅更新于被展示的特征值，视选择为外生）。从计算复杂度角度分析两类主体下的优化可行性，并通过美国住房调查数据进行校准实证。

Result: 1）为复杂型主体优化高亮策略在计算上不可行（即使简单离散二值设置）；2）为朴素型主体优化在最大带宽固定时是可行的；3）为复杂型设计的最优策略在朴素型面前可能表现任意差；4）实证表明高亮策略具有实际价值。

Conclusion: 高亮情境特定特征集合（而非固定特征集）是实现人机互补的实用且计算可行的方法，但需注意人类认知偏差对策略效果的影响，建议使用对认知假设更鲁棒的替代方案。

Abstract: Human decision-makers often face choices about complex cases with many potentially relevant features, but limited bandwidth to inspect and integrate all available information. In such settings, we study algorithms that highlight a small subset of case-specific features for human consideration, rather than producing a single prediction or recommendation. We model highlighting as a constrained information policy that selects a small number of features to reveal. A central issue is how humans interpret the algorithm's choice of features: a sophisticated agent correctly conditions on the selection rule, while a naive agent updates only on revealed feature values and treats the selection event as exogenous. We show that optimizing highlighting for sophisticated agents can be computationally intractable, even in simple discrete and binary settings, whereas optimizing for naive agents is tractable as long as the maximal bandwidth is fixed. We also show that a highlighting policy that is optimal for sophisticated agents can perform arbitrarily poorly when deployed to naive agents, motivating robust, implementable alternatives. We illustrate our framework in a calibrated empirical exercise based on the American Housing Survey. Overall, our results establish the value of highlighting a context-specific set of features rather than a fixed one as a practically appealing and computationally feasible tool for achieving human-algorithm complementarity.

</details>

### [120] [EgoMAGIC- An Egocentric Video Field Medicine Dataset for Training Perception Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22036)

Motivation: 为推进增强现实中虚拟助手在复杂医疗任务中的辅助能力，亟需一个高质量的第一人称医疗活动数据集。现有数据集缺乏针对医疗领域、自我中心视角且包含细粒度任务标注的资源。

Method: 使用头戴式立体相机（含集成音频）收集3,355个第一人称视频，覆盖50项医疗任务，每项至少50个标注视频。利用195万个标注训练40个YOLO模型，可检测124个医疗对象。在8项任务上构建动作检测基准，评估了三种模型。

Result: 最佳模型在动作检测任务上达到平均mAP 0.526。数据集包含1.95百万标注，训练了40个YOLO模型用于124个医疗对象的检测。

Conclusion: EgoMAGIC数据集不仅适用于动作检测，还可用于动作识别、目标识别与检测、错误检测等计算机视觉任务。数据集已在Zenodo上公开（DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.19239154），为医疗AI应用提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: This paper introduces EgoMAGIC (Medical Assistance, Guidance, Instruction, and Correction), an egocentric medical activity dataset collected as part of DARPA's Perceptually-enabled Task Guidance (PTG) program. This dataset comprises 3,355 videos of 50 medical tasks, with at least 50 labeled videos per task. The primary objective of the PTG program was to develop virtual assistants integrated into augmented reality headsets to assist users in performing complex tasks.
  To encourage exploration and research using this dataset, the medical training data has been released along with an action detection challenge focused on eight medical tasks. The majority of the videos were recorded using a head-mounted stereo camera with integrated audio. From this dataset, 40 YOLO models were trained using 1.95 million labels to detect 124 medical objects, providing a robust starting point for developers working on medical AI applications.
  In addition to introducing the dataset, this paper presents baseline results on action detection for the eight selected medical tasks across three models, with the best-performing method achieving average mAP 0.526. Although this paper primarily addresses action detection as the benchmark, the EgoMAGIC dataset is equally suitable for action recognition, object identification and detection, error detection, and other challenging computer vision tasks.
  The dataset is accessible via zenodo.org (DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.19239154).

### [121] [Anatomy-Aware Unsupervised Detection and Localization of Retinal Abnormalities in Optical Coherence Tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22139)
*Tania Haghighi,Sina Gholami,Hamed Tabkhi,Minhaj Nur Alam*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种无监督异常检测框架，通过学习健康视网膜的规范分布来检测OCT图像中的病变，无需专家标注，在多个数据集上取得优于基线方法的性能，并表现出良好的跨数据集泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决OCT影像分析中依赖昂贵、耗时的人工标注问题，以及监督深度学习方法因标注异常词汇有限而难以泛化到不同病理、设备和患者群体的困境。

Method: 基于离散潜在模型学习正常OCT结构模式，结合视网膜分层监督和结构化三元组学习分离健康与病理表征，通过重建差异实现图像级和像素级的异常检测与定位。

Result: Kermany数据集AUROC 0.799，优于VAE、VQVAE、VQGAN、f-AnoGAN基线；跨数据集Srinivasan AUROC 0.884；RETOUCH基准上无监督异常分割Dice 0.200、mIoU 0.117。

Conclusion: 该无监督框架有效降低了OCT分析对标注数据的依赖，具有良好的泛化能力和临床部署潜力，为视网膜疾病诊断提供了一种可行且鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Reliable automated analysis of Optical Coherence Tomography (OCT) imaging is crucial for diagnosing retinal disorders but faces a critical barrier: the need for expensive, labor-intensive expert annotations. Supervised deep learning models struggle to generalize across diverse pathologies, imaging devices, and patient populations due to their restricted vocabulary of annotated abnormalities. We propose an unsupervised anomaly detection framework that learns the normative distribution of healthy retinal anatomy without lesion annotations, directly addressing annotation efficiency challenges in clinical deployment. Our approach leverages a discrete latent model trained on normal B-scans to capture OCT-specific structural patterns. To enhance clinical robustness, we incorporate retinal layer-aware supervision and structured triplet learning to separate healthy from pathological representations, improving model reliability across varied imaging conditions. During inference, anomalies are detected and localized via reconstruction discrepancies, enabling both image and pixel-level identification without requiring disease-specific labels. On the Kermany dataset (AUROC: 0.799), our method substantially outperforms VAE, VQVAE, VQGAN, and f-AnoGAN baselines. Critically, cross-dataset evaluation on Srinivasan achieves AUROC 0.884 with superior generalization, demonstrating robust domain adaptation. On the external RETOUCH benchmark, unsupervised anomaly segmentation achieves competitive Dice (0.200) and mIoU (0.117) scores, validating reproducibility across institutions.

### [122] [All Eyes on the Workflow: Automated and Efficient Event Discovery from Video Streams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22476)
*Marco Pegoraro,Jonas Seng,Dustin Heller,Wil M. P. van der Aalst,Kristian Kersting*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SnapLog是一种从视频中提取事件数据的方法，利用图像嵌入将帧转换为特征向量，通过帧间相似矩阵进行时间分割，并使用广义少样本分类为视频片段分配标签，从而生成可被过程挖掘技术分析的事件日志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将视频帧通过图像嵌入转换为特征向量，利用帧间相似矩阵进行时间分割，再采用广义少样本分类为视频片段赋予标签，生成带时间戳的事件序列。

Result: 该方法生成的日志能够准确反映视频中的过程。

Conclusion: SnapLog成功弥合了视频数据与过程分析之间的鸿沟，使传统过程挖掘技术能够处理多模态数据。

Abstract: Disciplines such as business process management and process mining aid organizations by discovering insights about processes on the basis of recorded event data. However, an obstacle to process analysis is data multi-modality: for instance, data in video form are not directly interpretable as events. In this work, we present SnapLog, an approach to extract event data from videos by converting frames to feature vectors using image embeddings and performing temporal segmentation through frame-wise similarity matrices. A generalized few-shot classification is then used to assign labels to the video segments, yielding labeled, timestamped sub-sequences of frames that are interpretable as events. Conventional process mining techniques can be used to analyze the resulting data. We show that our approach produces logs that accurately reflect the process in the videos.

### [123] [Contrastive Semantic Projection: Faithful Neuron Labeling with Contrastive Examples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22477)
*Oussama Bouanani,Jim Berend,Wojciech Samek,Sebastian Lapuschkin,Maximilian Dreyer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出对比性神经元标注方法，通过引入对比样本（语义相似但激活低的输入）结合VLM和CLIP，显著提升了神经元标签的准确性和语义粒度，在黑色素瘤检测等任务中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经元标注方法依赖高激活样本，容易产生宽泛或误导性标签（关注偶然而非本质的视觉因素）。虽然FALCON引入了对比样本，但主要解决子空间层面的可解释性，缺乏可扩展的神经元级别标注方案。本文旨在将对比性解释扩展到神经元级别标注。

Method: 两阶段方法：(1) 候选标签生成：向VLM提供对比图像集（激活样本+对比样本），生成更具体更忠实的候选标签；(2) 标签分配：提出对比语义投影（CSP），将对比样本直接融入CLIP风格的评分与选择流程中，扩展了SemanticLens方法。

Result: 在大量实验和黑色素瘤检测案例研究中，对比性标注在忠实度和语义粒度上均优于当前最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: 对比样本是一种简单但强大且当前未被充分利用的神经元标注和分析组件，值得在可解释性研究中推广。

Abstract: Neuron labeling assigns textual descriptions to internal units of deep networks. Existing approaches typically rely on highly activating examples, often yielding broad or misleading labels by focusing on dominant but incidental visual factors. Prior work such as FALCON introduced contrastive examples -- inputs that are semantically similar to activating examples but elicit low activations -- to sharpen explanations, but it primarily addresses subspace-level interpretability rather than scalable neuron-level labeling. We revisit contrastive explanations for neuron-level labeling in two stages: (1) candidate label generation with vision language models (VLMs) and (2) label assignment with CLIP-like encoders. First, we show that providing contrastive image sets to VLMs yields candidate labels that are more specific and more faithful. Second, we introduce Contrastive Semantic Projection (CSP), an extension of SemanticLens that incorporates contrastive examples directly into its CLIP-based scoring and selection pipeline. Across extensive experiments and a case study on melanoma detection, contrastive labeling improves both faithfulness and semantic granularity over state-of-the-art baselines. Our results demonstrate that contrastive examples are a simple yet powerful and currently underutilized component of neuron labeling and analysis pipelines.

</details>


### [124] [Different Strokes for Different Folks: Writer Identification for Historical Arabic Manuscripts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22515)
*Hamza A. Abushahla,Ariel Justine N. Panopio,Layth Al-Khairulla,Mohamed I. AlHajri*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文基于Muharaf历史阿拉伯手稿数据集，扩展了作者标注（从28%提升至86.75%），提出带注意力的CNN模型进行行级和页级作者识别，在行级协议下达到99.05% Top-1准确率，页级协议下为78.61%，并首次建立了两种评估协议的基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿拉伯手稿承载着重要文化遗产，作者识别有助于来源追溯、真伪验证与历史分析。然而Muharaf数据集标注不完整，且缺乏统一的行级和页级评估基线，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 1) 人工验证并扩展Muharaf作者标签（从6,858行扩展到21,249行），纠正不一致并去除非手写文本；2) 提出基于CNN的注意力机制模型，支持封闭集作者识别；3) 对含两位作者的行建模为复合作者对类别；4) 在行级和页级两种协议下对14种配置进行消融实验。

Result: 行级协议：微调DenseNet201+注意力模型达到Top-1 99.05%、Top-5 99.73%、F1 97.44%。页级协议：最佳结果为Top-1 78.61%、Top-5 87.79%、F1 66.55%，揭示了页级线索对性能的影响。

Conclusion: 本文通过扩展标注和建立两种评估协议，为历史阿拉伯手稿作者识别提供了更清晰的基准，为历史学家和语言学家研究文化遗产文档提供了实用资源。

Abstract: Handwritten Arabic manuscripts preserve the Arab world's intellectual and cultural heritage, and writer identification supports provenance, authenticity verification, and historical analysis. Using the Muharaf dataset of historical Arabic manuscripts, we evaluate writer identification from individual line images and, to the best of our knowledge, provide the first baselines reported under both line-level and page-disjoint evaluation protocols. Since the dataset is only partially labeled for writer identification, we manually verified and expanded writer labels in the public portion from 6,858 (28.00%) to 21,249 lines (86.75%) out of 24,495 line images, correcting inconsistencies and removing non-handwritten text. After further filtering, we retained 18,987 lines (77.51%). We propose a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN)-based model with attention mechanisms for closed-set writer identification, including rare two-writer lines modeled as composite writer-pair classes. We benchmark fourteen configurations and conduct ablations across different feature extractors and training regimes. To assess generalization to unseen pages, the page-disjoint protocol assigns all lines from each page to a single split. Under the line-level protocol, a fine-tuned DenseNet201 with attention achieves 99.05% Top-1 accuracy, 99.73% Top-5 accuracy, and 97.44% F1-score. Under the more challenging page-disjoint protocol, the best observed results are 78.61% Top-1 accuracy, 87.79% Top-5 accuracy, and 66.55% F1-score, thus quantifying the impact of page-level cues. By expanding the Muharaf dataset's labeled subset and reporting both protocols, we provide a clearer benchmark and a practical resource for historians and linguists engaged with culturally and historically significant documents. The code and implementation details are available on GitHub.

</details>

### [125] [Audio Video Verbal Analysis (AVVA) for Capturing Classroom Dialogues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22043)
*Vivek Upadhyay,Amaresh Chakrabarti*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为AVVA（音频视频言语分析）的框架，用于分析课堂话语的多模态数据，该框架在十步方法论中嵌入了三角验证策略，并引入了一套综合验证方案（包括Phi Ceiling、Bootstrap置信区间、MTUP等）来解决时序观察研究中的关键挑战，通过对23小时课堂录音的应用展示了其可行性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 课堂话语分析正向音视频多模态数据发展，需要兼顾解释深度与计算可扩展性的分析方法。现有方法要么缺乏定量建模能力，要么过于依赖全量多模态特征，难以在两者间取得平衡。

Method: 从言语分析方法改编而来的AVVA框架，聚焦于逐字转录文本及必要的交互模态特征，将定性解释与定量建模相结合。框架包含十步方法论，以三角验证为核心设计策略，并针对低频率变量的Phi Ceiling问题（通过Base Rate Filtering）、估计不确定性（通过Bootstrap置信区间）及可修改时间单位问题（MTUP）等时序研究挑战，提出了四准则稳定性评估（符号一致性、置信区间重叠、零排除、量级稳定性）来分类变量对的粒度不变、尺度特异或多尺度结构。

Result: 通过对23小时课堂录音数据的应用，验证了AVVA框架的实际可行性，能够将丰富的课堂话语转化为可分析的数据集并产生有意义的洞察。

Conclusion: AVVA框架为将丰富的课堂话语转化为可分析的数据集提供了一条可扩展的路径，在定性深度与定量可扩展性之间实现了有效的平衡。

Abstract: Background: The classroom discourse analysis has been transformed by the growing use of audio-video multimodal data, which demands analytical methods that balance interpretive depth with computational scalability.
  Methods: This study introduces the Audio Video Verbal Analysis (AVVA) framework, adapted from the Verbal Analysis method to integrate qualitative interpretation with quantitative modelling. Unlike fully multimodal learning analytics approaches, AVVA focuses on verbatim transcripts with essential interactional modalities.
  Findings: The framework embeds triangulation as a core design strategy across ten methodological steps, strengthening validity and analytical rigour. A comprehensive validation scheme addresses fundamental challenges in temporal observational research: Phi Ceiling for low-frequency variables (via Base Rate Filtering), estimation uncertainty (via bootstrap confidence intervals), and the Modifiable Temporal Unit Problem, where measured associations depend on observational window size. Four-criterion stability assessment (sign consistency, confidence interval overlap, zero exclusion, magnitude stability) classifies variable pairs into interpretable patterns: grain-invariant, scale-specific, or multi-scale, etc. structures across temporal grain sizes. Its application to 23 hours of classroom recordings illustrates its practical viability and its potential to yield meaningful insights.
  Contribution: The framework thus provides a scalable pathway for transforming rich classroom discourse into analysable datasets.

</details>

### [126] [The Chase in Lean -- Crafting a Formal Library for Existential Rule Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22531)
*Lukas Gerlach*

Main category: cs.LO

TL;DR: 本文使用Lean定理证明器构建了一个关于存在规则（又称元组生成依赖）及其chase算法的形式化框架。作者讨论了将不同文献中chase定义翻译为Lean代码的设计决策，展示了chase结果是universal model的证明，概述了chase结果是core（当没有"alternative matches"时）的形式化过程，并将多种chase终止条件（如MFA）统一到一个共同框架中，同时增加了对规则中常量的支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 存在规则（tuple-generating dependencies）和chase算法在知识表示领域非常重要，但随着理论特性和优化研究的增长，验证正确性和重现证明变得困难，直觉有时会误导人。作者希望通过Lean定理证明器构建形式化框架，提供可验证、精确的证明，解决文献中chase定义细微差异带来的问题。

Method: 使用Lean（纯函数式编程语言和交互式定理证明器）构建形式化框架，围绕存在规则和chase算法。作者讨论了chase定义的细微差别及其在Lean中的翻译，通过形式化证明了chase结果是universal model，概述了在无"alternative matches"时chase是core的证明，并将Model-Faithful Acyclicity (MFA)等终止条件统一到框架中，同时扩展了对规则中常量的支持。

Result: 成功构建了Lean框架，形式化了存在规则和chase算法；证明了chase结果是universal model；概述了chase在无"alternative matches"时是core的形式化证明；将MFA等终止条件统一到框架中；增加了对规则中常量的支持。

Conclusion: Lean形式化框架能够精确、可靠地处理存在规则和chase算法中的复杂问题，包括不同定义间的细微差别、终止条件统一以及对常量的支持。这为未来更复杂的形式化推理奠定了基础，有助于验证正确性和重现证明。

Abstract: The chase is a sound, complete, but possibly non-terminating algorithm for reasoning with existential rules (aka. tuple-generating dependencies), a highly expressive knowledge representation language. Although the procedure appears simple, research on theoretical properties and optimization for practical implementations has grown to a point where verifying correctness and reproducing proofs becomes challenging and intuition can sometimes be misleading. Lean is a purely functional programming language and interactive theorem prover whose community actively develops formal libraries for mathematics (Mathlib) and computer science (CSLib). In this work, we present our own endeavor of crafting a Lean framework around existential rules and the chase. We discuss design decisions concerning the nuances of chase definitions commonly found in the literature and show how these translate into Lean. To illustrate the framework's capabilities using known results, we show that the result of a chase is a universal model and outline the formalization for proving that without so-called "alternative matches" it is even a core. Beyond existing literature, we unify sufficient chase termination conditions in the likeness of Model-Faithful Acyclicity (MFA) into a common framework while also adding support for constants in rules.

</details>

### [127] [Resource-Aware Layered Intrusion Detection Allocation Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22304)
*Ioan Pădurean,Béla Genge,Roland Bolboacă*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向异构网络的资源感知分层入侵检测分配模型，通过整数线性规划为每个设备分配监控深度（以太网到应用层），在资源预算、关键设备最低监控级别和受限设备最大可行性约束下，优化监控资源分配，并在六设备网络上验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异构网络中，高层协议监控能提升检测复杂攻击的能力，但会带来高昂的计算和存储成本。如何在有限资源下合理分配监控深度，同时兼顾设备重要性、攻击概率和检测率，是一个关键问题。

Method: 将问题建模为整数线性规划（ILP），为每个设备分配从以太网到应用层的单一监控深度，综合考虑设备重要性、攻击概率、各层检测率和监控成本，并施加全局资源预算、关键设备最低监控级别、受限设备（如IoT传感器）最大可行性约束，使用SCIP优化框架求解。

Result: 在包含六台设备的小型异构网络上求解该模型，得到的分配方案表明模型能够将监控资源集中于重要且高风险的设备，同时满足可行性约束和资源预算限制。

Conclusion: 所提出的资源感知分配模型能够有效平衡检测能力与资源开销，在异构网络场景下实现合理的分层监控资源分配，值得进一步扩展和验证。

Abstract: This paper proposes a resource-aware allocation model for layered intrusion detection in het erogeneous networks. Monitoring traffic at higher protocol layers improves the ability to detect sophisticated attacks, but it also increases computational and storage costs. The problem is formu lated as an integer linear program that assigns a single monitoring depth, ranging from Ethernet to the application layer, to each device, while accounting for device importance, attack probability, layer-dependent detection rates, and per-layer monitoring costs. The model further enforces a global resource budget, a minimum monitoring level for critical devices, and maximum-feasibility limits for constrained devices such as simple IoT sensors. The formulation is solved with the SCIP optimization framework on a small heterogeneous network of six devices, and the resulting allocation illustrates how the model concentrates monitoring effort on important and high-risk devices while respecting feasibility and budget constraints.

</details>

Abstract: In enterprise fraud detection, model accuracy alone is insufficient when insiders can tamper with audit logs or bypass approval workflows. This exposes a fundamental trust gap: *who audits the auditor?*
  We present a tamper-evident fraud detection system that anchors both ML predictions and workflow execution to an immutable blockchain ledger. Rather than using blockchain as passive storage, we enforce the entire approval process through smart contracts, ensuring that every transaction, prediction, and explanation is atomically recorded and cannot be retroactively modified. Our detection module achieves competitive accuracy (F1 = 0.895, PR-AUC = 0.974) while providing cryptographically verifiable decision trails that support regulatory auditability requirements (e.g., GDPR Article 22). We argue that this coupling creates a safety risk because model correctness, context awareness, and alignment cannot be assumed at execution time. We introduce Sovereign Agentic Loops (SAL), a control-plane architecture in which models emit structured intents with justifications, and the control plane validates those intents against true system state and policy before execution. SAL combines an obfuscation membrane, which limits model access to identity-sensitive state, with a cryptographically linked Evidence Chain for auditability and replay. We formalize SAL and show that, under the stated assumptions, it provides policy-bounded execution, identity isolation, and deterministic replay. In an OpenKedge prototype for cloud infrastructure, SAL blocks 93% of unsafe intents at the policy layer, rejects the remaining 7% via consistency checks, prevents unsafe executions in our benchmark, and adds 12.4 ms median latency.

FixV2W systematically analyzes historical remapping patterns and leverages hierarchical relationships within NVD and CWE data to predict more precise CWE mappings for vulnerabilities linked to Prohibited or Discouraged categories. For instance, for a model geared at uncovering unknown CVE-CWE mappings, FixV2W improves the Mean Reciprocal Rank (MRR) from 0.174 to 0.608. These results show that FixV2W is a promising approach to identify and thwart emerging threats.

These metrics are correlated with both accuracy degradation and data distribution shift as complementary drift indicators. The approach is evaluated across six malware families using fixed-interval and clustering-based windowing in family-vs-benign and family-vs-family settings, and compared against RIPPER and Transcendent baselines. Results show that fixed two-month windowing with feature-level Pearson correlation is the most reliable configuration, being the only one where all family pairs produce positive drift-accuracy correlations. The methods are complementary - no single approach dominates across all pairs.

In this work, we summarize the academic papers submitted in this field and develop a new adversarial malware generator for the ELF format. Using a variety of metrics, we thoroughly evaluated our generator and achieved an Evasion Rate of 67.74 % while changing the confidence of the malware detector by -0.50 in the mean case for the dataset used. In our approach, we chose MalConv as the target classifier. Using this classifier, we found that the most successful modifications used strings typical of benign files as a data source. We conducted a variety of experiments and concluded that the target classifier appears sensitive to strings at any location within the executable file.

### [135] [Concave Statistical Utility Maximization Bandits via Influence-Function Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22140)
*Matías Carrasco,Alejandro Cholaquidis*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究目标为长期奖励分布统计泛函（而非仅期望奖励）的随机多臂老虎机问题。在温和连续假设下，证明无限时域问题可简化为对平稳混合策略的优化；利用影响函数微积分从老虎机反馈中推导随机梯度估计器；提出截断单纯形上的熵镜像上升算法，通过乘法权重更新和影响函数的插件估计实现；建立将镜像上升优化误差与影响函数估计偏差分离的遗憾界；通过方差和Wasserstein目标进行数值实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的多臂老虎机研究主要聚焦于期望奖励最大化，但许多实际应用（如金融投资、风险管理）更关注奖励分布的统计特性（如方差、分位数、Wasserstein距离等）。本文旨在弥合这一鸿沟，将多臂老虎机框架从期望奖励推广到更一般的凹分布统计泛函。

Method: 1) 将问题规约为平稳混合策略上的凹函数优化；2) 利用影响函数微积分从老虎机反馈中构造随机梯度估计器；3) 在截断单纯形上设计熵镜像上升算法，结合乘法权重更新和影响函数的插件估计；4) 通过分离优化误差与估计偏差的方式建立遗憾界分析。

Result: 建立了将镜像上升优化误差与影响函数估计偏差分离的遗憾界；在方差和Wasserstein目标上进行了数值实验，对比了精确影响函数与插件估计影响函数实现的性能。

Conclusion: 本文为优化分布统计泛函的多臂老虎机问题提供了一个通用理论框架，证明了通过影响函数和镜像上升可有效求解，遗憾分析表明优化误差与估计偏差可分离处理，为更广泛的分布目标优化奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study stochastic multi-armed bandits in which the objective is a statistical functional of the long-run reward distribution, rather than expected reward alone. Under mild continuity assumptions, we show that the infinite-horizon problem reduces to optimizing over stationary mixed policies: each weight vector \(w\) on the simplex induces a mixture law \(P^w\), and performance is measured by the concave utility \(U(w)=\mathfrak U(P^w)\).
  For differentiable statistical utilities, we use influence-function calculus to derive stochastic gradient estimators from bandit feedback. This leads to an entropic mirror-ascent algorithm on a truncated simplex, implemented through multiplicative-weights updates and plug-in estimates of the influence function. We establish regret bounds that separate the mirror-ascent optimization error from the bias caused by estimating the influence function. The framework is developed for general concave distributional utilities and illustrated through variance and Wasserstein objectives, with numerical experiments comparing exact and plug-in influence-function implementations.

</details>


### [136] [Pliable rejection sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22385)
*Akram Erraqabi,Michal Valko,Alexandra Carpentier,Odalric-Ambrym Maillard*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于核估计的自适应拒绝采样方法（PRS），能高概率生成独立同分布样本，并保证接受样本数量。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拒绝采样因高拒绝率而受限，现有自适应方法要么只适用于特定分布，要么缺乏性能保证。

Method: 利用核估计器学习采样提议分布，在拒绝采样框架下进行自适应采样。

Result: 生成样本高概率为独立同分布且服从目标分布f；对接受样本数量提供了理论保证。

Conclusion: PRS在保持拒绝采样优势的同时，克服了高拒绝率和适应性差的限制。

Abstract: Rejection sampling is a technique for sampling from difficult distributions. However, its use is limited due to a high rejection rate. Common adaptive rejection sampling methods either work only for very specific distributions or without performance guarantees. In this paper, we present pliable rejection sampling (PRS), a new approach to rejection sampling, where we learn the sampling proposal using a kernel estimator. Since our method builds on rejection sampling, the samples obtained are with high probability i.i.d. and distributed according to f. Moreover, PRS comes with a guarantee on the number of accepted samples.

</details>


### [137] [Pack only the essentials: Adaptive dictionary learning for kernel ridge regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22386)
*Daniele Calandriello,Alessandro Lazaric,Michal Valko*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出SQUEAK算法，通过使用未归一化的岭回归杠杆分数（RLS）来改进INK-Estimate，在保证Nyström近似精度的同时，将空间复杂度降低到仅比精确RLS采样差一个常数因子，消除了对最大特征值的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核岭回归（KRR）在处理大规模数据时面临O(n²)的空间复杂度瓶颈，Nyström近似虽能降低复杂度，但均匀采样需要与数据相干性成比例的样本量，而精确的岭回归杠杆分数（RLS）采样本身也需要O(n²)空间。现有方法INK-Estimate虽能增量计算，但其空间复杂度依赖于最大特征值，最坏情况下仍为O(n)。

Method: 提出SQUEAK算法，使用未归一化的RLS替代归一化RLS，简化了算法流程，无需估计有效维度进行归一化，从而消除了INK-Estimate中对最大特征值的依赖，将空间复杂度降至仅比精确RLS采样差一个常数因子。

Result: SQUEAK算法在空间复杂度上仅比精确RLS采样差一个常数因子，避免了INK-Estimate中最坏情况O(n)的依赖，同时保持了Nyström近似的准确性。

Conclusion: SQUEAK通过使用未归一化RLS，在保持近似精度的同时显著降低了空间复杂度，为大规模KRR问题提供了更高效实用的解决方案。

Abstract: One of the major limits of kernel ridge regression (KRR) is that storing and manipulating the kernel matrix K_n for n samples requires O(n^2) space, which rapidly becomes unfeasible for large n. Nystrom approximations reduce the space complexity to O(nm) by sampling m columns from K_n. Uniform sampling preserves KRR accuracy (up to epsilon) only when m is proportional to the maximum degree of freedom of K_n, which may require O(n) columns for datasets with high coherence. Sampling columns according to their ridge leverage scores (RLS) gives accurate Nystrom approximations with m proportional to the effective dimension, but computing exact RLS also requires O(n^2) space.
  (Calandriello et al. 2016) propose INK-Estimate, an algorithm that processes the dataset incrementally and updates RLS, effective dimension, and Nystrom approximations on-the-fly. Its space complexity scales with the effective dimension but introduces a dependency on the largest eigenvalue of K_n, which in the worst case is O(n).
  In this paper we introduce SQUEAK, a new algorithm that builds on INK-Estimate but uses unnormalized RLS. As a consequence, the algorithm is simpler, does not need to estimate the effective dimension for normalization, and achieves a space complexity that is only a constant factor worse than exact RLS sampling.

</details>


### [138] [Conformalized Super Learner](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22391)
*Zhanli Wu,Fabrizio Leisen,Miguel-Angel Luque-Fernandez,F. Javier Rubio*

Main category: stat.ML

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超级学习器（SL）虽广泛用于点预测，但其区间预测方法多依赖渐近理论或计算密集型方法（如bootstrap），缺乏有限样本下的覆盖保证。因此需要一种既能保持SL灵活集成能力、又能提供可靠不确定性量化（预测区间）的方法。

Method: 将保形预测（CP）与超级学习器（SL）耦合：利用SL中的个体学习器权重，对学习器特定的保形分数进行加权多数投票，构建预测区间。该方法适用于可交换性、可交换性违反、异方差、稀疏性及分布异质性等场景。

Result: 模拟研究表明，保形化SL在有限样本下达到有效覆盖，性能与真实数据生成机制相当。在肌酐水平预测的真实应用中，集成了多种学习器（捕捉非线性、交互、稀疏性、异方差、离群鲁棒性）的SL展现出明显优势。

Conclusion: 保形化超级学习器为SL提供了一种原则性强、计算高效的预测区间构建方法，具有有限样本覆盖保证，并在复杂回归任务中表现优异，是SL不确定性量化的有力工具。

Abstract: The Super Learner (SL) is a widely used ensemble method that combines predictions from a library of learners based on their predictive performance. Interval predictions are of considerable practical interest because they allow uncertainty in predictions produced by an individual learner or an ensemble to be quantified. Several methods have been proposed for constructing interval predictions based on the SL, however, these approaches are typically justified using asymptotic arguments or rely on computationally intensive procedures such as the bootstrap. Conformal prediction (CP) is a machine learning framework for constructing prediction intervals with finite-sample and asymptotic coverage guarantees under mild conditions. We propose coupling CP with the SL through a natural construction that mirrors the original SL framework, using individual learner weights and combining learner-specific conformity scores via a weighted majority vote. We characterize the properties of the resulting SL-based prediction intervals for continuous outcomes. We cover settings under exchangeability, potential violations of exchangeability, and data-generating mechanisms exhibiting heteroscedasticity, sparsity, and other forms of distributional heterogeneity. A comprehensive simulation study shows that the conformalized SL achieves valid finite-sample coverage with competitive performance relative to the true data-generating mechanism. A central contribution of this work is an application to predicting creatinine levels using socio-demographic, biometric, and laboratory measurements. This example demonstrates the benefits of an ensemble with carefully selected learners designed to capture key aspects of complex regression functions, including non-linear effects, interactions, sparsity, heteroscedasticity, and robustness to outliers.R

### [139] [FedSPDnet: Geometry-Aware Federated Deep Learning with SPDnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22494)
*Thibault Pautrel,Florent Bouchard,Ammar Mian,Guillaume Ginolhac*

Main category: stat.ML
